    // Toggle the readable/runnable button for API reference cURL examples.
    function toggleCurl(id) {
      var e = document.getElementById(id);
      if (e.innerHTML == 'Show Readable') {
        e.innerHTML = 'Show Runnable';
        document.getElementById(id + '-read').style.display = 'block';
        document.getElementById(id + '-run').style.display = 'none';
      } else {
        e.innerHTML = 'Show Readable';
        document.getElementById(id + '-run').innerHTML =  document.getElementById(id + '-read').innerHTML.replace(/ *\n */g,' ');
        document.getElementById(id + '-read').style.display = 'none';
        document.getElementById(id + '-run').style.display = 'block';
      }
      return(false);
    }
  </script>

     <h1 id="introduction">Introduction</h1> 
     <div class="annotation-block"> 
      <div class="annotation-block--left"> 
       <aside class="notice">
         The IBM Watson™ AlchemyLanguage service is being deprecated. As of 
        <b>April 7, 2017</b>, it will no longer be possible to create a new instance of the service on Bluemix. Existing service instances will continue to be supported until 
        <b>Mar 7, 2018</b>. 
       </aside> 
       <p> The IBM Watson™ AlchemyLanguage service is a collection of text analysis functions that derive semantic information from your content. You can input text, HTML, or a public URL and leverage sophisticated natural language processing techniques to get a quick high-level understanding of your content and obtain detailed insights such as sentiment for detected entities and keywords. See a video overview of the service <a href="https://youtu.be/pQZObFvou40">here</a>. </p> 
       <p> Before HTML documents or webpages are analyzed, AlchemyLanguage removes ads, headers, and other unwanted text by default, leaving only the most important source text for the analysis. </p> 
       <p> Maximum size of requested or posted HTML documents: 600 KB<br> Maximum size of source text after page cleaning: 50 KB </p> 
       <p>Watson Developer Cloud SDKs: </p>
       <ul> 
        <li><a href="https://github.com/watson-developer-cloud/node-sdk">Node SDK</a></li> 
        <li><a href="https://github.com/watson-developer-cloud/java-sdk">Java SDK</a></li> 
        <li><a href="https://github.com/watson-developer-cloud/python-sdk">Python SDK</a></li> 
        <li><a href="https://github.com/watson-developer-cloud/ios-sdk">iOS SDK</a></li> 
       </ul> 
       <p></p> 
      </div> 
      <div class="annotation-block--right"> 
       <div class="method-curl"> 
        <p class="code-header">API Endpoint</p> 
        <!-- Update the service-url --> 
        <pre><code class="nohighlight">https://gateway-a.watsonplatform.net/calls</code></pre> 
        <p class="code-header">Important: If you have Bluemix Dedicated, this may not be your service endpoint. Double check your endpoint URL on the Service Credentials page in your instance of the AlchemyLanguage Service on Bluemix.</p> 
        <!-- Update the endpoint with your service name --> 
       </div> 
       <div class="method-node"> 
        <p class="code-header">Node</p> 
        <pre><code class="lang-bash">npm install watson-developer-cloud</code></pre> 
       </div> 
       <div class="method-java"> 
        <p class="code-header">Maven</p> 
        <!--
   Check to make sure that maven and gradle refer to the latest
   version of the SDKs. See the release notes in the repos
   where they live. These versions are current as of 6-Jan-2016.
--> 
        <pre><code class="lang-xml">&lt;dependency&gt;
  &lt;groupId&gt;com.ibm.watson.developer_cloud&lt;/groupId&gt;
  &lt;artifactId&gt;java-sdk&lt;/artifactId&gt;
  &lt;version&gt;3.0.0-RC1&lt;/version&gt;
&lt;/dependency&gt;</code></pre> 
        <p class="code-header">Gradle</p> 
        <pre><code>compile 'com.ibm.watson.developer_cloud:java-sdk:3.0.0-RC1'</code></pre> 
       </div> 
       <div class="method-python"> 
        <p class="code-header">Python</p> 
        <pre><code class="lang-bash">pip install --upgrade watson-developer-cloud</code></pre> 
       </div> 
      </div> 
     </div> 
     <h1 id="authentication">Authentication</h1> 
     <div class="annotation-block"> 
      <div class="annotation-block--left"> 
       <p> You authenticate to the AlchemyLanguage API by passing an API key as a query parameter in each call. </p> 
       <p> To get an API key, you'll need to <a href="https://console.ng.bluemix.net/registration/">sign up for IBM Bluemix</a>. After you create an account: </p>
       <ul> 
        <li>Log in to Bluemix and go to the <a href="https://console.ng.bluemix.net/catalog/services/alchemyapi/" target="_blank">AlchemyAPI service page</a>.</li> 
        <li>Click the "Create" button.</li> 
        <li>Click the "Service Credentials" button from the AlchemyAPI page in your <a href="https://console.ng.bluemix.net/dashboard/">Bluemix dashboard</a> to view your API key.</li> 
       </ul> 
       <p></p> 
      </div> 
      <div class="annotation-block--right"> 
       <pre class="method-curl"><code class="bash">
curl "https://gateway-a.watsonplatform.net/calls/url/URLGetAuthors?apikey=API_KEY&amp;url=www.ibm.com"
            </code></pre> 
       <pre class="method-node"><code class="javascript">
var watson = require('watson-developer-cloud');
var alchemy_language = watson.alchemy_language({
  api_key: 'API_KEY'
});
            </code></pre> 
       <pre class="method-java"><code class="java">
AlchemyLanguage service = new AlchemyLanguage();
service.setApiKey("API_KEY");
            </code></pre> 
       <pre class="method-python"><code class="python">
import json
from watson_developer_cloud import AlchemyLanguageV1

alchemy_language = AlchemyLanguageV1(api_key='API_KEY')
            </code></pre> 
      </div> 
     </div> 
     <!-- methods: begin --> 
     <h1 id="methods">Methods</h1> 
     <!-- The focus of the methods is not on endpoint, but on action. So sort the methods by logical action, and make sure your descriptions are action verbs beyond GET, POST etc if needed --> 
     <h2 id="combined-call">Combined Call</h2> 
     <div class="method-curl annotation-block--left combined-call inputToggles"> 
      <span class="inputToggle" onclick="toggleMethod('combined-call', 'alchemy-html', this)">HTML</span> 
      <span class="inputToggle inputSelect" onclick="toggleMethod('combined-call', 'alchemy-url', this)">URL</span> 
      <span class="inputToggle" onclick="toggleMethod('combined-call', 'alchemy-text', this)">Text</span> 
      <p class="combined-call alchemy-html">Analyze an HTML file with multiple text analysis operations.</p> 
      <p class="combined-call alchemy-url">Analyze a webpage with multiple text analysis operations.</p> 
      <p class="combined-call alchemy-text">Analyze plain text with multiple text analysis operations.</p> 
     </div> 
     <p class="method-node method-java method-python">Analyze text, HTML, or webpage content with multiple text analysis operations.</p> 
     <p> For example, if you want to get entity and keyword information from the same source, you can do it in a single call. Specify any of the available methods in the <tt>extract</tt> parameter to enable them in the analysis. Any charges that apply to the individual methods used will be reflected in the combined request. </p> 
     <p> Any parameters for the <tt>extract</tt> methods can also be passed. You can refer to their corresponding sections of the reference to see the options that are available. For example, you can enable targeted sentiment information for entities and keywords by passing <tt>sentiment=1</tt>. Since this parameter incurs additional transaction charges and applies to both entities and keywords, the request will incur 2 additional transaction charges. </p> 
     <pre class="method-curl nohighlight"><code class="combined-call alchemy-html">POST /html/HTMLGetCombinedData</code><code class="combined-call alchemy-url">GET /url/URLGetCombinedData<br>POST /url/URLGetCombinedData</code><code class="combined-call alchemy-text">POST /text/TextGetCombinedData</code></pre> 
     <pre class="method-node"><code class="javascript">combined(parameters, callback)</code></pre> 
     <pre class="method-python"><code class="python">combined(parameter=value,...)</code></pre> 
     <h3 id="request_combined-call">Request</h3> 
     <div class="method-curl"> 
      <div class="combined-call alchemy-url annotation-block"> 
       <div class="annotation-block--left"> 
        <table class="align-right-1 unwrap-1 unwrap-2"> 
         <thead> 
          <tr> 
           <th>Parameter</th> 
           <th>Type</th> 
           <th>Description</th> 
          </tr> 
         </thead> 
         <tbody> 
          <tr> 
           <td>apikey</td> 
           <td>query</td> 
           <td>(<strong>Required</strong>) Your API key</td> 
          </tr> 
          <tr> 
           <td>url</td> 
           <td>query</td> 
           <td>(<strong>Required</strong>) HTTP URL</td> 
          </tr> 
          <tr> 
           <td>extract</td> 
           <td>query</td> 
           <td>Comma separated list of any of the following methods: 
            <ul> 
             <li>authors</li> 
             <li>concepts (default)</li> 
             <li>dates</li> 
             <li>doc-emotion</li> 
             <li>entities (default)</li> 
             <li>feeds</li> 
             <li>keywords (default)</li> 
             <li>pub-date</li> 
             <li>relations</li> 
             <li>typed-rels</li> 
             <li>doc-sentiment</li> 
             <li>taxonomy (default)</li> 
             <li>title</li> 
            </ul> </td> 
          </tr> 
          <tr> 
           <td>outputMode</td> 
           <td>query</td> 
           <td><tt>json</tt> or <tt>xml</tt> (default)</td> 
          </tr> 
          <tr> 
           <td>showSourceText</td> 
           <td>query</td> 
           <td>Set this to 1 to include the source text in the response</td> 
          </tr> 
          <tr> 
           <td>jsonp</td> 
           <td>query</td> 
           <td>Desired JSONP callback (requires <tt>outputMode</tt> to be set to <tt>json</tt>)</td> 
          </tr> 
         </tbody> 
        </table> 
       </div> 
       <!-- request curl -->

})

var parameters = {

  sentiment: 1,
  maxRetrieve: 1,
  url: 'https://www.ibm.com/us-en/'

     <h2 id="concepts">Concepts</h2> 
     <div class="method-curl annotation-block--left concepts inputToggles"> 
      <span class="inputToggle" onclick="toggleMethod('concepts', 'alchemy-html', this)">HTML</span> 
      <span class="inputToggle inputSelect" onclick="toggleMethod('concepts', 'alchemy-url', this)">URL</span> 
      <span class="inputToggle" onclick="toggleMethod('concepts', 'alchemy-text', this)">Text</span> 
      <p class="concepts alchemy-html">Extract concepts from an HTML document.</p> 
      <p class="concepts alchemy-url">Extract concepts from a webpage.</p> 
      <p class="concepts alchemy-text">Extract concepts from plain text.</p> 
     </div> 
     <p class="method-node method-java method-python"> Extract concepts from a webpage, HTML, or plain text. </p> 
     <p>Supported languages: English, Spanish</p> 
     <pre class="method-curl nohighlight"><code class="concepts alchemy-html">POST /html/HTMLGetRankedConcepts</code><code class="concepts alchemy-url">POST /url/URLGetRankedConcepts</code><code class="concepts alchemy-text">POST /text/TextGetRankedConcepts</code></pre> 
     <pre class="method-node"><code class="javascript">concepts(parameters, callback)</code></pre> 
     <pre class="method-python"><code class="python">concepts(parameter=value,...)</code></pre> 
     <h3 id="request_concepts">Request</h3> 
     <!-- update the id to match the method name, but in lower case --> 
     <!-- parameters --> 
     <div class="method-curl"> 
      <div class="annotation-block concepts alchemy-html"> 
       <div class="annotation-block--left"> 
        <!-- If there are no parameters in the call, remove the table and include this paragraph:
            <p>No arguments</p>
            --> 
        <table class="align-right-1 unwrap-1">

           <th>Type</th> 
           <th>Description</th>

           <td>query</td>

           <td>Input here will appear as the <tt>url</tt> value in the response.</td> 
          </tr>

           <td>query</td> 
           <td>Maximum number of concepts to extract (default = 8, maximum = 50)</td> 
          </tr>

           <td>query</td>

           <td>query</td> 
           <td>Set this to 1 to include the source text in the response</td> 
          </tr> 
          <tr> 
           <td>cquery</td> 
           <td>query</td> 
           <td>A <a href="../../../doc/alchemylanguage/visual_constraints.html">visual constraints query</a> to apply to the web page. Required when <tt>sourceText</tt> is set to <tt>cquery</tt></td> 
          </tr> 
          <tr> 
           <td>xpath</td> 
           <td>query</td> 
           <td>An XPath query to apply to the web page. Required when <tt>sourceText</tt> is set to one of the XPath values</td> 
          </tr> 
          <tr> 
           <td>sourceText</td> 
           <td>query</td> 
           <td>How to obtain the source text from the webpage. Possible values:<br> 
            <table class="descriptionTable"> 
             <tbody>
              <tr> 
               <td><tt>cleaned_or_raw</tt> (default)</td> 
               <td>Removes website elements such as links, ads, etc. If cleaning fails, raw web page text is used</td> 
              </tr> 
              <tr>
               <td><tt>cleaned</tt></td> 
               <td>Removes website elements such as links, ads, etc.</td> 
              </tr>
              <tr> 
               <td><tt>raw</tt></td> 
               <td>Uses raw web page text with no cleaning</td> 
              </tr> 
              <tr> 
               <td><tt>cquery</tt></td> 
               <td>Uses the <a href="../../../doc/alchemylanguage/visual_constraints.html">visual constraints query</a> that you specify in the <tt>cquery</tt> parameter</td> 
              </tr> 
              <tr> 
               <td><tt>xpath</tt></td> 
               <td>Uses the XPath query that you specify in the <tt>xpath</tt> parameter</td> 
              </tr> 
              <tr> 
               <td><tt>xpath_or_raw</tt></td> 
               <td>Uses the results of an XPath query that you specify in the <tt>xpath</tt> parameter, falling back to plain text if the XPath query returns nothing</td> 
              </tr> 
              <tr> 
               <td><tt>cleaned_and_xpath</tt></td> 
               <td>Uses the results of an XPath query on cleaned web page text</td> 
              </tr> 
             </tbody>
            </table> </td> 
          </tr> 
         </tbody> 
        </table>

     <h2 id="date_extraction">Date Extraction</h2> 
     <div class="method-curl annotation-block--left date_extraction inputToggles"> 
      <span class="inputToggle" onclick="toggleMethod('date_extraction', 'alchemy-html', this)">HTML</span> 
      <span class="inputToggle inputSelect" onclick="toggleMethod('date_extraction', 'alchemy-url', this)">URL</span> 
      <span class="inputToggle" onclick="toggleMethod('date_extraction', 'alchemy-text', this)">Text</span> 
      <p class="date_extraction alchemy-html">Extract dates from an HTML document.</p> 
      <p class="date_extraction alchemy-url">Extract dates from a webpage.</p> 
      <p class="date_extraction alchemy-text">Extract dates from plain text.</p> 
     </div> 
     <p class="method-node method-java method-python"> Extract dates from a webpage, HTML, or plain text. </p> 
     <p> Supported languages: English </p> 
     <pre class="method-curl nohighlight"><code class="date_extraction alchemy-html">POST /html/HTMLExtractDates</code><code class="date_extraction alchemy-url">GET /url/URLExtractDates<br>POST /url/URLExtractDates</code><code class="date_extraction alchemy-text">POST /text/TextExtractDates</code></pre> 
     <pre class="method-node"><code class="javascript">dates(parameters, callback)</code></pre> 
     <pre class="method-python"><code class="python">dates(parameter=value,...)</code></pre> 
     <h3 id="request_date_extraction date_extraction">Request</h3> 
     <!-- update the id to match the method name, but in lower case --> 
     <!-- parameters --> 
     <div class="method-curl"> 
      <div class="annotation-block date_extraction alchemy-html"> 
       <div class="annotation-block--left"> 
        <!-- If there are no parameters in the call, remove the table and include this paragraph:
            <p>No arguments</p>
            --> 
        <table class="align-right-1 unwrap-1"> 
         <thead> 
          <tr> 
           <th>Parameter</th> 
           <th>Type</th> 
           <th>Description</th> 
          </tr> 
         </thead> 
         <tbody> 
          <tr> 
           <td>apikey</td> 
           <td>query</td> 
           <td>(<strong>Required</strong>) Your API key</td> 
          </tr> 
          <tr> 
           <td>html</td> 
           <td>query</td> 
           <td>(<strong>Required</strong>) HTML content (must be URL encoded)</td> 
          </tr> 
          <tr> 
           <td>anchorDate</td> 
           <td>query</td> 
           <td>The date to use as "today" when interpreting phrases in the text like "next tuesday."<br>Format: <tt>yyyy-mm-dd hh:mm:ss</tt></td> 
          </tr> 
          <tr> 
           <td>outputMode</td> 
           <td>query</td> 
           <td><tt>json</tt>, <tt>rdf</tt>, <tt>xml</tt> (default), <tt>rel-tag</tt>, or <tt>rel-tag-raw</tt></td> 
          </tr> 
          <tr> 
           <td>jsonp</td> 
           <td>query</td> 
           <td>JSONP callback (requires <tt>outputMode</tt> to be set to json)</td> 
          </tr> 
          <tr>
           <td>showSourceText</td> 
           <td>query</td> 
           <td>Set this to 1 to include the source text in the response</td> 
          </tr> 
          <tr> 
           <td>url</td> 
           <td>query</td> 
           <td>Input here will appear as the <tt>url</tt> value in the response.</td> 
          </tr> 
         </tbody> 
        </table> 
       </div> 
       <!-- request curl --> 
       <div class="annotation-block--right"> 
        <p class="code-header">Example request</p> 
        <pre class="method-curl"><code class="lang-bash">

        <pre><code class="javascript">
var watson = require('watson-developer-cloud');
var alchemy_language = watson.alchemy_language({
  api_key: 'API_KEY'
})

var parameters = {
  text: 'Set a reminder for my appointment next Tuesday',
  anchorDate: '2016-03-22 00:00:00'
};

alchemy_language.dates(parameters, function (err, response) {
  if (err)
    console.log('error:', err);
  else
    console.log(JSON.stringify(response, null, 2));
});</code></pre>

     <h3 id="response_date_extraction">Response</h3> 
     <!-- update the id to match the method name, but in lower case --> 
     <div class="annotation-block date_extraction"> 
      <div class="annotation-block--left"> 
       <table class="align-right-1 unwrap-1"> 
        <thead> 
         <tr> 
          <th>Name</th> 
          <th>Description</th> 
         </tr> 
        </thead> 
        <tbody> 
         <tr> 
          <td>status</td> 
          <td><tt>OK</tt> or <tt>ERROR</tt><br>Indicates whether the request was successful</td> 
         </tr> 
         <tr> 
          <td>url</td> 
          <td>HTTP url sent in the input</td> 
         </tr> 
         <tr> 
          <td>language</td> 
          <td>Detected language of the source text (text with fewer than 15 characters is assumed to be English)</td> 
         </tr> 
         <tr> 
          <td>text</td> 
          <td>Source text of the document. Appears when <tt>showSourceText</tt> is set to 1</td> 
         </tr> 
         <tr> 
          <td>dates</td> 
          <td>Array of extracted date objects, each containing a date in <tt>yyyymmddThhmmss</tt> format and text from the source that corresponds to the date</td> 
         </tr> 
        </tbody> 
       </table>

     <h2 id="emotion_analysis">Emotion Analysis</h2> 
     <div class="method-curl annotation-block--left emotion_analysis inputToggles"> 
      <span class="inputToggle" onclick="toggleMethod('emotion_analysis', 'alchemy-html', this)">HTML</span> 
      <span class="inputToggle inputSelect" onclick="toggleMethod('emotion_analysis', 'alchemy-url', this)">URL</span> 
      <span class="inputToggle" onclick="toggleMethod('emotion_analysis', 'alchemy-text', this)">Text</span> 
      <p class="emotion_analysis alchemy-html">Detect emotions implied in the text of an HTML document.</p> 
      <p class="emotion_analysis alchemy-url">Detect emotions implied in the text on a webpage.</p> 
      <p class="emotion_analysis alchemy-text">Detect emotions implied in plain text.</p> 
     </div> 
     <p class="method-node method-java method-python"> Detect emotions implied in plain text, on a webpage, or in HTML content. </p> 
     <p> Supported languages: English </p> 
     <pre class="method-curl nohighlight"><code class="emotion_analysis alchemy-html">POST /html/HTMLGetEmotion</code><code class="emotion_analysis alchemy-url">GET /url/URLGetEmotion<br>POST /url/URLGetEmotion</code><code class="emotion_analysis alchemy-text">POST /text/TextGetEmotion</code></pre> 
     <pre class="method-node"><code class="javascript">emotion(parameters, callback)</code></pre> 
     <pre class="method-python"><code class="python">emotion(parameter=value,...)</code></pre> 
     <h3 id="request_emotion_analysis emotion_analysis">Request</h3> 
     <!-- update the id to match the method name, but in lower case --> 
     <!-- parameters --> 
     <div class="method-curl"> 
      <div class="annotation-block emotion_analysis alchemy-html"> 
       <div class="annotation-block--left"> 
        <!-- If there are no parameters in the call, remove the table and include this paragraph:
            <p>No arguments</p>
            --> 
        <table class="align-right-1 unwrap-1"> 
         <thead> 
          <tr> 
           <th>Parameter</th> 
           <th>Type</th> 
           <th>Description</th> 
          </tr> 
         </thead> 
         <tbody> 
          <tr> 
           <td>apikey</td> 
           <td>query</td> 
           <td>(<strong>Required</strong>) Your API key</td> 
          </tr> 
          <tr> 
           <td>html</td> 
           <td>query</td> 
           <td>(<strong>Required</strong>) HTML content (must be URL encoded)</td> 
          </tr> 
          <tr> 
           <td>url</td> 
           <td>query</td> 
           <td>Input here will appear as the <tt>url</tt> value in the response.</td> 
          </tr> 
          <tr> 
           <td>outputMode</td> 
           <td>query</td> 
           <td><tt>json</tt> or <tt>xml</tt> (default)</td> 
          </tr> 
          <tr> 
           <td>jsonp</td> 
           <td>query</td> 
           <td>JSONP callback (requires <tt>outputMode</tt> to be set to json)</td> 
          </tr> 
          <tr> 
           <td>showSourceText</td> 
           <td>query</td> 
           <td>Set this to 1 to include the source text in the response</td> 
          </tr> 
          <tr> 
           <td>cquery</td> 
           <td>query</td> 
           <td>A <a href="../../../doc/alchemylanguage/visual_constraints.html">visual constraints query</a> to apply to the web page. Required when <tt>sourceText</tt> is set to <tt>cquery</tt></td> 
          </tr> 
          <tr> 
           <td>xpath</td> 
           <td>query</td> 
           <td>An XPath query to apply to the web page. Required when <tt>sourceText</tt> is set to one of the XPath values</td> 
          </tr> 
          <tr> 
           <td>sourceText</td> 
           <td>query</td> 
           <td>How to obtain the source text from the webpage. Possible values:<br> 
            <table class="descriptionTable"> 
             <tbody>
              <tr> 
               <td><tt>cleaned_or_raw</tt> (default)</td> 
               <td>Removes website elements such as links, ads, etc. If cleaning fails, raw web page text is used</td> 
              </tr> 
              <tr>
               <td><tt>cleaned</tt></td> 
               <td>Removes website elements such as links, ads, etc.</td> 
              </tr>
              <tr> 
               <td><tt>raw</tt></td> 
               <td>Uses raw web page text with no cleaning</td> 
              </tr> 
              <tr> 
               <td><tt>cquery</tt></td> 
               <td>Uses the <a href="../../../doc/alchemylanguage/visual_constraints.html">visual constraints query</a> that you specify in the <tt>cquery</tt> parameter</td> 
              </tr> 
              <tr> 
               <td><tt>xpath</tt></td> 
               <td>Uses the XPath query that you specify in the <tt>xpath</tt> parameter</td> 
              </tr> 
              <tr> 
               <td><tt>xpath_or_raw</tt></td> 
               <td>Uses the results of an XPath query that you specify in the <tt>xpath</tt> parameter, falling back to plain text if the XPath query returns nothing</td> 
              </tr> 
              <tr> 
               <td><tt>cleaned_and_xpath</tt></td> 
               <td>Uses the results of an XPath query on cleaned web page text</td> 
              </tr> 
             </tbody>
            </table> </td> 
          </tr> 
         </tbody> 
        </table> 
       </div>

})

var parameters = {
  url: 'http://www.charliechaplin.com/en/synopsis/articles/29-The-Great-Dictator-s-Speech'
};

alchemy_language.emotion(parameters, function (err, response) {
  if (err)
    console.log('error:', err);
  else
    console.log(JSON.stringify(response, null, 2));
});</code></pre> 
       </div> 
      </div>

        <table class="align-right-1 unwrap-1"> 
         <thead> 
          <tr> 
           <th>Parameter</th> 
           <th>Type</th> 
           <th>Description</th> 
          </tr> 
         </thead> 
         <tbody> 
          <tr> 
           <td>api_key<span class="req"></span></td> 
           <td>string</td> 
           <td>Your API key</td> 
          </tr> 
          <tr> 
           <td>html, url, text<span class="req"></span></td> 
           <td>string</td> 
           <td>One of these is required. Pass HTML content in <tt>html</tt>, a public facing URL in <tt>url</tt>, or plain text in <tt>text</tt></td> 
          </tr> 
          <tr> 
           <td>show_source_text</td> 
           <td>integer</td> 
           <td>Set this to <tt>1</tt> to include the source text in the response</td> 
          </tr> 
          <tr> 
           <td>constraint_query</td> 
           <td>string</td> 
           <td>A <a href="../../../doc/alchemylanguage/visual_constraints.html">visual constraints query</a> to apply to the web page. Required when <tt>source_text</tt> is set to <tt>cquery</tt></td> 
          </tr> 
          <tr> 
           <td>xpath_query</td> 
           <td>integer</td> 
           <td>An XPath query to apply to the web page. Required when <tt>source_text</tt> is set to one of the XPath values</td> 
          </tr> 
          <tr> 
           <td>source_text</td> 
           <td>query</td> 
           <td>How to obtain the source text from the webpage. Possible values:<br> 
            <table class="descriptionTable"> 
             <tbody>
              <tr> 
               <td><tt>cleaned_or_raw</tt> (default)</td> 
               <td>Removes website elements such as links, ads, etc. If cleaning fails, raw web page text is used</td> 
              </tr> 
              <tr>
               <td><tt>cleaned</tt></td> 
               <td>Removes website elements such as links, ads, etc.</td> 
              </tr>
              <tr> 
               <td><tt>raw</tt></td> 
               <td>Uses raw web page text with no cleaning</td> 
              </tr> 
              <tr> 
               <td><tt>cquery</tt></td> 
               <td>Uses the <a href="../../../doc/alchemylanguage/visual_constraints.html">visual constraints query</a> that you specify in the <tt>cquery</tt> parameter</td> 
              </tr> 
              <tr> 
               <td><tt>xpath</tt></td> 
               <td>Uses the XPath query that you specify in the <tt>xpath</tt> parameter</td> 
              </tr> 
              <tr> 
               <td><tt>xpath_or_raw</tt></td> 
               <td>Uses the results of an XPath query that you specify in the <tt>xpath</tt> parameter, falling back to plain text if the XPath query returns nothing</td> 
              </tr> 
              <tr> 
               <td><tt>cleaned_and_xpath</tt></td> 
               <td>Uses the results of an XPath query on cleaned web page text</td> 
              </tr> 
             </tbody>
            </table> </td> 
          </tr> 
         </tbody> 
        </table> 
       </div>

import json
from watson_developer_cloud import AlchemyLanguageV1

alchemy_language = AlchemyLanguageV1(api_key='API_KEY')
print(json.dumps(

     <h2 id="targeted_emotion">Targeted Emotion</h2> 
     <div class="method-curl annotation-block--left targeted_emotion inputToggles"> 
      <span class="inputToggle" onclick="toggleMethod('targeted_emotion', 'alchemy-html', this)">HTML</span> 
      <span class="inputToggle inputSelect" onclick="toggleMethod('targeted_emotion', 'alchemy-url', this)">URL</span> 
      <span class="inputToggle" onclick="toggleMethod('targeted_emotion', 'alchemy-text', this)">Text</span> 
      <p class="targeted_emotion alchemy-html">Detect emotions directed toward targeted phrases in an HTML document.</p> 
      <p class="targeted_emotion alchemy-url">Detect emotions directed toward targeted phrases on a webpage.</p> 
      <p class="targeted_emotion alchemy-text">Detect emotions directed toward targeted phrases in text.</p> 
     </div> 
     <p class="method-node method-java method-python"> Detect emotions directed toward targeted phrases in your content. </p> 
     <p> Targeted Emotion searches your content for up to 20 targets, and uses context to analyze emotions associated with each phrase. You can analyze emotions for <a href="#keywords">keywords</a> and <a href="#entities">entities</a> by passing an <tt>emotion=1</tt> parameter when you use the respective API methods, or when you extract keywords and entities in a <a href="#combined-call">Combined Call</a>. </p> 
     <p> Supported languages: English </p> 
     <pre class="method-curl nohighlight"><code class="targeted_emotion alchemy-html">POST /html/HTMLGetTargetedEmotion</code><code class="targeted_emotion alchemy-url">GET /url/URLGetTargetedEmotion<br>POST /url/URLGetTargetedEmotion</code><code class="targeted_emotion alchemy-text">POST /text/TextGetTargetedEmotion</code></pre> 
     <pre class="method-node"><code class="javascript">emotion(parameters, callback)</code></pre> 
     <h3 id="request_targeted_emotion targeted_emotion">Request</h3> 
     <!-- parameters --> 
     <div class="method-curl">

     <h3 id="response_targeted_emotion">Response</h3> 
     <!-- update the id to match the method name, but in lower case --> 
     <div class="annotation-block"> 
      <div class="annotation-block--left"> 
       <table class="align-right-1 unwrap-1"> 
        <thead> 
         <tr> 
          <th>Name</th> 
          <th>Description</th> 
         </tr> 
        </thead> 
        <tbody> 
         <tr> 
          <td>status</td> 
          <td><tt>OK</tt> or <tt>ERROR</tt><br>Indicates whether the request was successful</td> 
         </tr> 
         <tr> 
          <td>url</td> 
          <td>HTTP URL that was passed in the input</td> 
         </tr> 
         <tr> 
          <td>language</td> 
          <td>Detected language of the source text (text with fewer than 15 characters is assumed to be English)</td> 
         </tr> 
         <tr> 
          <td>text</td> 
          <td>Source text of the document. Appears when <tt>showSourceText</tt> is set to 1</td> 
         </tr> 
         <tr> 
          <td>results</td> 
          <td>Array of result objects. Each result contains the text of the detected target, and an object containing scores for anger, disgust, fear, joy, and sadness. The higher the score, the more likely the emotion is associated with the target phrase.</td> 
         </tr> 
        </tbody> 
       </table> 
      </div> 
      <div class="annotation-block--right">

  "totalTransactions": "1",
  "language": "english",
  "results": [
    {
      "emotions": {
        "anger": "0.156846",
        "disgust": "0.299988",
        "fear": "0.367965",
        "joy": "0.250093",
        "sadness": "0.438412"
      },
      "text": "Clinton"
    },
    {
      "emotions": {
        "anger": "0.116643",
        "disgust": "0.309158",
        "fear": "0.367396",
        "joy": "0.22114",
        "sadness": "0.55768"
      },
      "text": "Trump"
    }
  ]
}
              </code></pre> 
        <pre class="targeted_emotion alchemy-text"><code class="json">

     <h2 id="entities">Entities</h2> 
     <div class="method-curl annotation-block--left entities inputToggles"> 
      <span class="inputToggle" onclick="toggleMethod('entities', 'alchemy-html', this)">HTML</span> 
      <span class="inputToggle inputSelect" onclick="toggleMethod('entities', 'alchemy-url', this)">URL</span> 
      <span class="inputToggle" onclick="toggleMethod('entities', 'alchemy-text', this)">Text</span> 
      <p class="entities alchemy-html">Extract entities from an HTML document.</p> 
      <p class="entities alchemy-url">Extract entities from a webpage.</p> 
      <p class="entities alchemy-text">Extract entities from plain text.</p> 
     </div> 
     <p class="method-node method-java method-python"> Extract entities from a webpage, HTML, or plain text. </p> 
     <p> Get the full list of standard entity types (sheet 1) and subtypes (sheet 2): <a download="alchemy-language-entity-types.xls" href="https://github.com/watson-developer-cloud/doc-tutorial-downloads/blob/master/alchemy-language/alchemy-language-entity-types.xls?raw=true">XLS</a> </p> 
     <p> To tailor results for your domain, you can create your own <a href="../../../doc/alchemylanguage/customizing.html">custom models</a> for entity extraction with Watson Knowledge Studio. </p> 
     <p> Supported languages: English, French, German, Italian, Portuguese, Russian, Spanish, Swedish </p> 
     <pre class="method-curl nohighlight"><code class="entities alchemy-html">POST /html/HTMLGetRankedNamedEntities</code><code class="entities alchemy-url">GET /url/URLGetRankedNamedEntities<br>POST /url/URLGetRankedNamedEntities</code><code class="entities alchemy-text">POST /text/TextGetRankedNamedEntities</code></pre> 
     <pre class="method-node"><code class="javascript">entities(parameters, callback)</code></pre> 
     <pre class="method-python"><code class="python">entities(parameter=value,...)</code></pre> 
     <h3 id="request_entities entities">Request</h3> 
     <!-- update the id to match the method name, but in lower case --> 
     <!-- parameters --> 
     <div class="method-curl"> 
      <div class="annotation-block entities alchemy-html"> 
       <div class="annotation-block--left"> 
        <!-- If there are no parameters in the call, remove the table and include this paragraph:
            <p>No arguments</p>
            --> 
        <table class="align-right-1 unwrap-1"> 
         <thead> 
          <tr> 
           <th>Parameter</th> 
           <th>Type</th> 
           <th>Description</th> 
          </tr> 
         </thead> 
         <tbody> 
          <tr> 
           <td>apikey</td> 
           <td>query</td> 
           <td>(<strong>Required</strong>) Your API key</td> 
          </tr> 
          <tr> 
           <td>html</td> 
           <td>query</td> 
           <td>(<strong>Required</strong>) HTML content (must be URL encoded)</td> 
          </tr> 
          <tr> 
           <td>maxRetrieve</td> 
           <td>query</td> 
           <td>Maximum number of entities to return (default = 50)</td> 
          </tr> 
          <tr> 
           <td>model</td> 
           <td>query</td> 
           <td>Specify a custom model ID here to override the default Alchemy entity extraction model. You can also choose from the following public models: 
            <ul> 
             <li>en-news: trained on English news content</li> 
             <li>es-news: trained on Spanish news content</li> 
             <li>ar-news: trained on Arabic news content</li> 
            </ul> <b>Note: </b> input text is truncated to 5 KB for custom models calls </td> 
          </tr> 
          <tr> 
           <td>outputMode</td> 
           <td>query</td> 
           <td><tt>json</tt> or <tt>xml</tt> (default)</td> 
          </tr> 
          <tr> 
           <td>jsonp</td> 
           <td>query</td> 
           <td>JSONP callback (requires <tt>outputMode</tt> to be set to json)</td> 
          </tr> 
          <tr> 
           <td>url</td> 
           <td>query</td> 
           <td>Input here will appear as the <tt>url</tt> value in the response.</td> 
          </tr> 
          <tr> 
           <td>coreference</td> 
           <td>query</td> 
           <td>Set this to 0 to treat coreferences as separate entities (coreferences are resolved into detected entities by default)</td> 
          </tr> 
          <tr> 
           <td>disambiguate</td> 
           <td>query</td> 
           <td>Set this to 0 to hide entity disambiguation information in the response </td> 
          </tr> 
          <tr> 
           <td>knowledgeGraph</td> 
           <td>query</td> 
           <td>Set this to 1 to include knowledge graph information in the results<br><strong>This incurs an additional transaction charge</strong></td> 
          </tr> 
          <tr> 
           <td>linkedData</td> 
           <td>query</td> 
           <td>Set this to 0 to hide <a href="#linked-data">Linked Data</a> content links in the response</td> 
          </tr> 
          <tr> 
           <td>quotations</td> 
           <td>query</td> 
           <td>Set this to 1 to include quotations that are linked to detected entities</td> 
          </tr> 
          <tr> 
           <td>emotion</td> 
           <td>query</td> 
           <td>Set this to 1 to analyze emotions associated with each detected entity<br><strong>This incurs an additional transaction charge</strong> </td> 
          </tr> 
          <tr> 
           <td>sentiment</td> 
           <td>query</td> 
           <td>Set this to 1 to analyze the sentiment towards each detected entity<br><strong>This incurs an additional transaction charge</strong> </td> 
          </tr> 
          <tr> 
           <td>showSourceText</td> 
           <td>query</td> 
           <td>Set this to 1 to include the source text in the response</td> 
          </tr> 
          <tr> 
           <td>structuredEntities</td> 
           <td>query</td> 
           <td>Set this to 0 to ignore structured entities, such as Quantity, EmailAddress, TwitterHandle, Hashtag, and IPAddress</td> 
          </tr> 
          <tr> 
           <td>cquery</td> 
           <td>query</td> 
           <td>A <a href="../../../doc/alchemylanguage/visual_constraints.html">visual constraints query</a> to apply to the web page. Required when <tt>sourceText</tt> is set to <tt>cquery</tt></td> 
          </tr> 
          <tr> 
           <td>xpath</td> 
           <td>query</td> 
           <td>An XPath query to apply to the web page. Required when <tt>sourceText</tt> is set to one of the XPath values</td> 
          </tr> 
          <tr> 
           <td>sourceText</td> 
           <td>query</td> 
           <td>How to obtain the source text from the webpage. Possible values:<br> 
            <table class="descriptionTable"> 
             <tbody>
              <tr> 
               <td><tt>cleaned_or_raw</tt> (default)</td> 
               <td>Removes website elements such as links, ads, etc. If cleaning fails, raw web page text is used</td> 
              </tr> 
              <tr>
               <td><tt>cleaned</tt></td> 
               <td>Removes website elements such as links, ads, etc.</td> 
              </tr>
              <tr> 
               <td><tt>raw</tt></td> 
               <td>Uses raw web page text with no cleaning</td> 
              </tr> 
              <tr> 
               <td><tt>cquery</tt></td> 
               <td>Uses the <a href="../../../doc/alchemylanguage/visual_constraints.html">visual constraints query</a> that you specify in the <tt>cquery</tt> parameter</td> 
              </tr> 
              <tr> 
               <td><tt>xpath</tt></td> 
               <td>Uses the XPath query that you specify in the <tt>xpath</tt> parameter</td> 
              </tr> 
              <tr> 
               <td><tt>xpath_or_raw</tt></td> 
               <td>Uses the results of an XPath query that you specify in the <tt>xpath</tt> parameter, falling back to plain text if the XPath query returns nothing</td> 
              </tr> 
              <tr> 
               <td><tt>cleaned_and_xpath</tt></td> 
               <td>Uses the results of an XPath query on cleaned web page text</td> 
              </tr> 
             </tbody>
            </table> </td> 
          </tr> 
         </tbody> 
        </table> 
       </div> 
       <!-- request curl --> 
       <div class="annotation-block--right">

            </code></pre>

               <td><tt>xpath</tt></td> 
               <td>Uses the XPath query that you specify in the <tt>xpath</tt> parameter</td> 
              </tr> 
              <tr> 
               <td><tt>xpath_or_raw</tt></td> 
               <td>Uses the results of an XPath query that you specify in the <tt>xpath</tt> parameter, falling back to plain text if the XPath query returns nothing</td> 
              </tr> 
              <tr> 
               <td><tt>cleaned_and_xpath</tt></td> 
               <td>Uses the results of an XPath query on cleaned web page text</td> 
              </tr> 
             </tbody>
            </table> </td> 
          </tr> 
         </tbody> 
        </table> 
       </div> 
       <div class="annotation-block--right"> 
        <p class="code-header">Example Request</p> 
        <pre><code class="javascript">
var watson = require('watson-developer-cloud');
var alchemy_language = watson.alchemy_language({
  api_key: 'API_KEY'
})

var parameters = {
  url: 'http://www-03.ibm.com/press/us/en/pressrelease/49384.wss'
};

alchemy_language.entities(parameters, function (err, response) {
  if (err)
    console.log('error:', err);
  else
    console.log(JSON.stringify(response, null, 2));
});</code></pre>

      <div class="entities annotation-block"> 
       <div class="annotation-block--left"> 
        <table class="align-right-1 unwrap-1"> 
         <thead> 
          <tr> 
           <th>Parameter</th> 
           <th>Type</th> 
           <th>Description</th> 
          </tr> 
         </thead> 
         <tbody> 
          <tr> 
           <td>api_key<span class="req"></span></td> 
           <td>string</td> 
           <td>Your API key</td> 
          </tr> 
          <tr> 
           <td>html, url, text<span class="req"></span></td> 
           <td>string</td> 
           <td>One of these is required. Pass HTML content in <tt>html</tt>, a public facing URL in <tt>url</tt>, or plain text in <tt>text</tt></td> 
          </tr> 
          <tr> 
           <td>max_items</td> 
           <td>integer</td> 
           <td>Maximum number of entities to return (default = 50)</td> 
          </tr> 
          <tr> 
           <td>model</td> 
           <td>string</td> 
           <td>Specify a custom model ID here to override the default Alchemy entity extraction model. You can also choose from the following public models: 
            <ul> 
             <li>en-news: trained on English news content</li> 
             <li>es-news: trained on Spanish news content</li> 
             <li>ar-news: trained on Arabic news content</li> 
            </ul> <b>Note: </b> input text is truncated to 5 KB for custom models calls </td> 
          </tr> 
          <tr> 
           <td>outputMode</td> 
           <td>string</td> 
           <td><tt>xml</tt> or <tt>json</tt> (default)</td> 
          </tr> 
          <tr> 
           <td>coreference</td> 
           <td>integer</td> 
           <td>Set this to 0 to treat coreferences as separate entities (coreferences are resolved into detected entities by default)</td> 
          </tr> 
          <tr> 
           <td>show_source_text</td> 
           <td>integer</td> 
           <td>Set this to 1 to include the source text in the response</td> 
          </tr> 
          <tr> 
           <td>linked_data</td> 
           <td>integer</td> 
           <td>Set this to 0 to hide <a href="#linked-data">Linked Data</a> content links in the response</td> 
          </tr> 
          <tr> 
           <td>quotations</td> 
           <td>integer</td> 
           <td>Set this to 1 to include quotations that are linked to detected entities</td> 
          </tr> 
          <tr> 
           <td>emotion</td> 
           <td>integer</td> 
           <td>Set this to 1 to analyze emotions associated with each detected entity<br><strong>This incurs an additional transaction charge</strong> </td> 
          </tr> 
          <tr> 
           <td>sentiment</td> 
           <td>integer</td> 
           <td>Set this to 1 to analyze the sentiment towards each detected entity. <strong>This incurs an additional transaction charge</strong> </td> 
          </tr> 
         </tbody> 
        </table> 
       </div>

  indent=2))

     <h2 id="feed_detection">Feed Detection</h2> 
     <div class="method-curl annotation-block--left feed_detection inputToggles"> 
      <span class="inputToggle" onclick="toggleMethod('feed_detection', 'alchemy-html', this)">HTML</span> 
      <span class="inputToggle inputSelect" onclick="toggleMethod('feed_detection', 'alchemy-url', this)">URL</span> 
      <p class="feed_detection alchemy-html">Extract RSS/ATOM feed links from an HTML document.</p> 
      <p class="feed_detection alchemy-url">Extract RSS/ATOM feed links from a webpage.</p> 
     </div> 
     <p class="method-node method-java method-python"> Extract RSS/ATOM feed links from a webpage or HTML. </p> 
     <pre class="method-curl nohighlight"><code class="feed_detection alchemy-html">POST /html/HTMLGetFeedLinks</code><code class="feed_detection alchemy-url">GET /url/URLGetFeedLinks<br>POST /url/URLGetFeedLinks</code></pre> 
     <pre class="method-node"><code class="javascript">feeds(parameters, callback)</code></pre> 
     <pre class="method-python"><code class="python">feeds(parameter=value,...)</code></pre>-

     <h2 id="keywords">Keywords</h2> 
     <div class="method-curl annotation-block--left keywords inputToggles"> 
      <span class="inputToggle" onclick="toggleMethod('keywords', 'alchemy-html', this)">HTML</span> 
      <span class="inputToggle inputSelect" onclick="toggleMethod('keywords', 'alchemy-url', this)">URL</span> 
      <span class="inputToggle" onclick="toggleMethod('keywords', 'alchemy-text', this)">Text</span> 
      <p class="keywords alchemy-html">Extract keywords from an HTML document.</p> 
      <p class="keywords alchemy-url">Extract keywords from a webpage.</p> 
      <p class="keywords alchemy-text">Extract keywords from plain text.</p> 
     </div> 
     <p class="method-node method-java method-python"> Extract keywords from a webpage, HTML, or plain text. </p> 
     <p> Supported languages: English, French, German, Italian, Portuguese, Russian, Spanish, Swedish </p> 
     <pre class="method-curl nohighlight"><code class="keywords alchemy-html">POST /html/HTMLGetRankedKeywords</code><code class="keywords alchemy-url">GET /url/URLGetRankedKeywords<br>POST /url/URLGetRankedKeywords</code><code class="keywords alchemy-text">POST /text/TextGetRankedKeywords</code></pre> 
     <pre class="method-node"><code class="javascript">keywords(parameters, callback)</code></pre> 
     <pre class="method-python"><code class="python">keywords(parameter=value,...)</code></pre> 
     <h3 id="request_keywords keywords">Request</h3> 
     <!-- update the id to match the method name, but in lower case --> 
     <!-- parameters --> 
     <div class="method-curl"> 
      <div class="annotation-block keywords alchemy-html"> 
       <div class="annotation-block--left"> 
        <!-- If there are no parameters in the call, remove the table and include this paragraph:
            <p>No arguments</p>
            --> 
        <table class="align-right-1 unwrap-1"> 
         <thead> 
          <tr> 
           <th>Parameter</th> 
           <th>Type</th> 
           <th>Description</th> 
          </tr> 
         </thead> 
         <tbody> 
          <tr> 
           <td>apikey</td> 
           <td>query</td> 
           <td>(<strong>Required</strong>) Your API key</td> 
          </tr> 
          <tr> 
           <td>html</td> 
           <td>query</td> 
           <td>(<strong>Required</strong>) HTML content (must be URL encoded)</td> 
          </tr> 
          <tr> 
           <td>outputMode</td> 
           <td>query</td> 
           <td><tt>json</tt> or <tt>xml</tt> (default)</td> 
          </tr> 
          <tr> 
           <td>jsonp</td> 
           <td>query</td> 
           <td>JSONP callback (requires <tt>outputMode</tt> to be set to json)</td> 
          </tr> 
          <tr> 
           <td>url</td> 
           <td>query</td> 
           <td>Input here will appear as the <tt>url</tt> value in the response.</td> 
          </tr> 
          <tr> 
           <td>maxRetrieve</td> 
           <td>query</td> 
           <td>Maximum number of keywords to return (default = 50)</td> 
          </tr> 
          <tr> 
           <td>knowledgeGraph</td> 
           <td>query</td> 
           <td>Set this to 1 to include knowledge graph information in the results<br><strong>This incurs an additional transaction charge</strong></td> 
          </tr> 
          <tr> 
           <td>emotion</td> 
           <td>query</td> 
           <td>Set this to 1 to analyze emotions associated with each detected entity<br><strong>This incurs an additional transaction charge</strong> </td> 
          </tr> 
          <tr> 
           <td>sentiment</td> 
           <td>query</td> 
           <td>Set this to 1 to analyze the sentiment towards each detected entity<br><strong>This incurs an additional transaction charge</strong> </td> 
          </tr> 
          <tr> 
           <td>showSourceText</td> 
           <td>query</td> 
           <td>Set this to 1 to include the source text in the response</td> 
          </tr> 
          <tr> 
           <td>cquery</td> 
           <td>query</td> 
           <td>A <a href="../../../doc/alchemylanguage/visual_constraints.html">visual constraints query</a> to apply to the web page. Required when <tt>sourceText</tt> is set to <tt>cquery</tt></td> 
          </tr> 
          <tr> 
           <td>xpath</td> 
           <td>query</td> 
           <td>An XPath query to apply to the web page. Required when <tt>sourceText</tt> is set to one of the XPath values</td> 
          </tr> 
          <tr> 
           <td>sourceText</td> 
           <td>query</td> 
           <td>How to obtain the source text from the webpage. Possible values:<br> 
            <table class="descriptionTable"> 
             <tbody>
              <tr> 
               <td><tt>cleaned_or_raw</tt> (default)</td> 
               <td>Removes website elements such as links, ads, etc. If cleaning fails, raw web page text is used</td> 
              </tr> 
              <tr>
               <td><tt>cleaned</tt></td> 
               <td>Removes website elements such as links, ads, etc.</td> 
              </tr>
              <tr> 
               <td><tt>raw</tt></td> 
               <td>Uses raw web page text with no cleaning</td> 
              </tr> 
              <tr> 
               <td><tt>cquery</tt></td> 
               <td>Uses the <a href="../../../doc/alchemylanguage/visual_constraints.html">visual constraints query</a> that you specify in the <tt>cquery</tt> parameter</td> 
              </tr> 
              <tr> 
               <td><tt>xpath</tt></td> 
               <td>Uses the XPath query that you specify in the <tt>xpath</tt> parameter</td> 
              </tr> 
              <tr> 
               <td><tt>xpath_or_raw</tt></td> 
               <td>Uses the results of an XPath query that you specify in the <tt>xpath</tt> parameter, falling back to plain text if the XPath query returns nothing</td> 
              </tr> 
              <tr> 
               <td><tt>cleaned_and_xpath</tt></td> 
               <td>Uses the results of an XPath query on cleaned web page text</td> 
              </tr> 
             </tbody>
            </table> </td> 
          </tr> 
         </tbody> 
        </table> 
       </div>

              </tr> 
              <tr> 
               <td><tt>cleaned_and_xpath</tt></td> 
               <td>Uses the results of an XPath query on cleaned web page text</td> 
              </tr> 
             </tbody>
            </table> </td>

     <h3 id="response_keywords">Response</h3> 
     <!-- update the id to match the method name, but in lower case --> 
     <div class="annotation-block"> 
      <div class="annotation-block--left"> 
       <table class="align-right-1 unwrap-1"> 
        <thead> 
         <tr> 
          <th>Name</th> 
          <th>Description</th> 
         </tr> 
        </thead> 
        <tbody> 
         <tr> 
          <td>status</td> 
          <td><tt>OK</tt> or <tt>ERROR</tt><br>Indicates whether the request was successful</td> 
         </tr> 
         <tr> 
          <td>url</td> 
          <td>HTTP URL that was passed in the input</td> 
         </tr> 
         <tr> 
          <td>language</td> 
          <td>Detected language of the source text (text with fewer than 15 characters is assumed to be English)</td> 
         </tr> 
         <tr> 
          <td>keywords</td> 
          <td>Array of detected keyword objects 
           <table class="descriptionTable"> 
            <tbody>
             <tr> 
              <td>relevance</td> 
              <td>Relevance score for a detected keyword (<tt>0.0</tt> - <tt>1.0</tt>, <tt>1.0</tt> = most relevant)</td> 
             </tr> 
             <tr> 
              <td>text</td> 
              <td>Detected keyword text</td> 
             </tr> 
            </tbody>
           </table> </td> 
         </tr> 
         <tr> 
          <td>knowledgeGraph</td> 
          <td>Path through the knowledge graph to the appropriate keyword. Returned when the <tt>knowledgeGraph</tt> parameter is set to <tt>1</tt></td> 
         </tr> 
         <tr> 
          <td>sentiment</td> 
          <td><a href="#sentiment">Sentiment Analysis</a> results for the detected entity. Set <tt>sentiment</tt> to <tt>1</tt> to return this information 
           <table class="descriptionTable"> 
            <tbody>
             <tr> 
              <td>type</td> 
              <td>Sentiment polarity: <tt>positive</tt>, <tt>negative</tt>, or <tt>neutral</tt></td> 
             </tr> 
             <tr> 
              <td>score</td> 
              <td>Sentiment strength (<tt>0.0</tt> == neutral)</td> 
             </tr> 
             <tr> 
              <td>mixed</td> 
              <td><tt>1</tt> indicates that the sentiment is both positive and negative</td> 
             </tr> 
            </tbody>
           </table> </td> 
         </tr> 
        </tbody> 
       </table>

     <!-- method: begin --> 
     <h2 id="language">Language Detection</h2> 
     <div class="method-curl annotation-block--left language inputToggles"> 
      <span class="inputToggle" onclick="toggleMethod('language', 'alchemy-html', this)">HTML</span> 
      <span class="inputToggle inputSelect" onclick="toggleMethod('language', 'alchemy-url', this)">URL</span> 
      <span class="inputToggle" onclick="toggleMethod('language', 'alchemy-text', this)">Text</span> 
      <p class="language alchemy-html">Detect the language of an HTML document.</p> 
      <p class="language alchemy-url">Detect the language of a webpage.</p> 
      <p class="language alchemy-text">Detect the language of plain text.</p> 
     </div> 
     <p class="method-node method-java method-python"> Detect the language of a webpage, HTML, or plain text. </p> 
     <p> Language detection runs automatically in each API call. This method provides more information about the detected language. For language detection to work best, make sure your source text has at least 100 characters. If you're having trouble with language detection, you can pass the <tt>language</tt> parameter in any call to manually specify the language of your content. </p> 
     <p>See the complete list of detectable languages <a href="#language-support">here</a></p> 
     <pre class="method-curl nohighlight"><code class="language alchemy-html">POST /html/HTMLGetLanguage</code><code class="language alchemy-url">GET /url/URLGetLanguage<br>POST /url/URLGetLanguage</code><code class="language alchemy-text">POST /text/TextGetLanguage</code></pre> 
     <pre class="method-node"><code class="javascript">language(parameters, callback)</code></pre> 
     <pre class="method-python"><code class="python">language(parameter=value,...)</code></pre>

           <td>(<strong>Required</strong>) Your API key</td> 
          </tr> 
          <tr> 
           <td>url</td> 
           <td>query</td> 
           <td>(<strong>Required</strong>) HTTP URL</td> 
          </tr> 
          <tr> 
           <td>outputMode</td> 
           <td>query</td> 
           <td><tt>json</tt> or <tt>xml</tt> (default)</td> 
          </tr> 
          <tr> 
           <td>jsonp</td> 
           <td>query</td> 
           <td>JSONP callback (requires <tt>outputMode</tt> to be set to json)</td> 
          </tr> 
          <tr> 
           <td>showSourceText</td> 
           <td>query</td> 
           <td>Set this to 1 to include the source text in the response</td> 
          </tr> 
          <tr> 
           <td>cquery</td> 
           <td>query</td> 
           <td>A <a href="../../../doc/alchemylanguage/visual_constraints.html">visual constraints query</a> to apply to the web page. Required when <tt>sourceText</tt> is set to <tt>cquery</tt></td> 
          </tr> 
          <tr> 
           <td>xpath</td> 
           <td>query</td> 
           <td>An XPath query to apply to the web page. Required when <tt>sourceText</tt> is set to one of the XPath values</td> 
          </tr> 
          <tr> 
           <td>sourceText</td> 
           <td>query</td> 
           <td>How to obtain the source text from the webpage. Possible values:<br> 
            <table class="descriptionTable"> 
             <tbody>
              <tr> 
               <td><tt>cleaned_or_raw</tt> (default)</td> 
               <td>Removes website elements such as links, ads, etc. If cleaning fails, raw web page text is used</td> 
              </tr> 
              <tr>
               <td><tt>cleaned</tt></td> 
               <td>Removes website elements such as links, ads, etc.</td> 
              </tr>
              <tr> 
               <td><tt>raw</tt></td> 
               <td>Uses raw web page text with no cleaning</td> 
              </tr> 
              <tr> 
               <td><tt>cquery</tt></td> 
               <td>Uses the <a href="../../../doc/alchemylanguage/visual_constraints.html">visual constraints query</a> that you specify in the <tt>cquery</tt> parameter</td> 
              </tr> 
              <tr> 
               <td><tt>xpath</tt></td> 
               <td>Uses the XPath query that you specify in the <tt>xpath</tt> parameter</td> 
              </tr> 
              <tr> 
               <td><tt>xpath_or_raw</tt></td> 
               <td>Uses the results of an XPath query that you specify in the <tt>xpath</tt> parameter, falling back to plain text if the XPath query returns nothing</td> 
              </tr> 
              <tr> 
               <td><tt>cleaned_and_xpath</tt></td> 
               <td>Uses the results of an XPath query on cleaned web page text</td> 
              </tr> 
             </tbody>
            </table> </td> 
          </tr> 
         </tbody> 
        </table> 
       </div> 
       <!-- request curl --> 
       <div class="annotation-block--right"> 
        <p class="code-header">Example request</p> 
        <pre class="method-curl"><code class="lang-bash">
curl -X POST -d "outputMode=json" -d "url=http://www.ibm.com/us-en/" "https://gateway-a.watsonplatform.net/calls/url/URLGetLanguage?apikey=%API_KEY%"
            </code></pre> 
       </div> 
      </div>

     <h2 id="Microformats">Microformats</h2> 
     <div class="method-curl annotation-block--left microformats inputToggles"> 
      <span class="inputToggle" onclick="toggleMethod('microformats', 'alchemy-html', this)">HTML</span> 
      <span class="inputToggle inputSelect" onclick="toggleMethod('microformats', 'alchemy-url', this)">URL</span> 
      <p class="microformats alchemy-html">Extract microformats from an HTML document.</p> 
      <p class="microformats alchemy-url">Extract microformats from a webpage.</p> 
     </div> 
     <p class="method-node method-java method-python"> Extract microformats from a webpage or HTML. </p> 
     <p><a href="#supported-microformats">Supported microformats</a></p> 
     <pre class="method-curl nohighlight"><code class="microformats alchemy-html">POST /html/HTMLGetMicroformatData</code><code class="microformats alchemy-url">GET /url/URLGetMicroformatData<br>POST /url/URLGetMicroformatData</code></pre> 
     <pre class="method-node"><code class="javascript">microformats(parameters, callback)</code></pre> 
     <pre class="method-python"><code class="python">microformats(parameter=value,...)</code></pre>

     <h2 id="publication_date">Publication Date</h2> 
     <div class="method-curl annotation-block--left publication_date inputToggles"> 
      <span class="inputToggle" onclick="toggleMethod('publication_date', 'alchemy-html', this)">HTML</span> 
      <span class="inputToggle inputSelect" onclick="toggleMethod('publication_date', 'alchemy-url', this)">URL</span> 
      <p class="publication_date alchemy-html">Get the publication date of an HTML document.</p> 
      <p class="publication_date alchemy-url">Get the publication date of a webpage.</p> 
     </div> 
     <p class="method-node method-java method-python"> Get the publication date of a webpage or HTML document. </p> 
     <pre class="method-curl nohighlight"><code class="publication_date alchemy-html">POST /html/HTMLGetPubDate</code><code class="publication_date alchemy-url">GET /url/URLGetPubDate<br>POST /url/URLGetPubDate</code></pre> 
     <pre class="method-node"><code class="javascript">publicationDate(parameters, callback)</code></pre> 
     <pre class="method-python"><code class="python">publication_date(parameter=value,...)</code></pre> 
     <h3 id="request_publication_date publication_date">Request</h3> 
     <!-- update the id to match the method name, but in lower case --> 
     <!-- parameters --> 
     <div class="method-curl"> 
      <div class="annotation-block publication_date alchemy-html"> 
       <div class="annotation-block--left"> 
        <!-- If there are no parameters in the call, remove the table and include this paragraph:

            --> 
        <table class="align-right-1 unwrap-1">

           <th>Parameter</th> 
           <th>Type</th> 
           <th>Description</th> 
          </tr> 
         </thead>

          <tr> 
           <td>apikey</td> 
           <td>query</td> 
           <td>(<strong>Required</strong>) Your API key</td> 
          </tr> 
          <tr> 
           <td>html</td> 
           <td>query</td> 
           <td>(<strong>Required</strong>) HTML content (must be URL encoded)</td> 
          </tr> 
          <tr> 
           <td>outputMode</td> 
           <td>query</td> 
           <td><tt>json</tt> or <tt>xml</tt> (default)</td> 
          </tr> 
          <tr> 
           <td>jsonp</td> 
           <td>query</td> 
           <td>JSONP callback (requires <tt>outputMode</tt> to be set to json)</td> 
          </tr> 
          <tr> 
           <td>url</td> 
           <td>query</td> 
           <td>Input here will appear as the <tt>url</tt> value in the response.</td> 
          </tr> 
         </tbody> 
        </table> 
       </div>

            </code></pre>

     <div class="method-node"> 
      <div class="publication_date annotation-block"> 
       <div class="annotation-block--left"> 
        <table class="align-right-1 unwrap-1"> 
         <thead> 
          <tr> 
           <th>Parameter</th> 
           <th>Type</th> 
           <th>Description</th> 
          </tr> 
         </thead> 
         <tbody> 
          <tr> 
           <td>apikey<span class="req"></span></td> 
           <td>string</td> 
           <td>Your API key</td> 
          </tr> 
          <tr> 
           <td>html, url, text<span class="req"></span></td> 
           <td>string</td> 
           <td>One of these is required. Pass HTML content in <tt>html</tt>, a public facing URL in <tt>url</tt>, or plain text in <tt>text</tt></td> 
          </tr> 
          <tr> 
           <td>outputMode</td> 
           <td>string</td> 
           <td><tt>xml</tt> or <tt>json</tt> (default)</td> 
          </tr> 
          <tr> 
           <td>showSourceText</td> 
           <td>integer</td> 
           <td>Set this to <tt>1</tt> to include the source text in the response</td> 
          </tr> 
         </tbody> 
        </table> 
       </div> 
       <div class="annotation-block--right"> 
        <p class="code-header">Example Request</p> 
        <pre><code class="javascript">
var watson = require('watson-developer-cloud');
var alchemy_language = watson.alchemy_language({
  api_key: 'API_KEY'
})

var parameters = {
  url: 'https://www.whitehouse.gov/the-press-office/2016/03/19/weekly-address-president-obamas-supreme-court-nomination'
};

alchemy_language.publicationDate(parameters, function (err, response) {
  if (err)
    console.log('error:', err);
  else
    console.log(JSON.stringify(response, null, 2));
});</code></pre>

import json
from watson_developer_cloud import AlchemyLanguageV1

alchemy_language = AlchemyLanguageV1(api_key='API_KEY')
print(json.dumps(
  alchemy_language.publication_date(
    url='https://www.whitehouse.gov/the-press-office/2016/03/19/weekly-address-president-obamas-supreme-court-nomination'),
  indent=2))
</code></pre>

     <h3 id="response_publication_date">Response</h3> 
     <!-- update the id to match the method name, but in lower case --> 
     <div class="annotation-block publication_date"> 
      <div class="annotation-block--left"> 
       <table class="align-right-1 unwrap-1"> 
        <thead> 
         <tr> 
          <th>Name</th> 
          <th>Description</th> 
         </tr> 
        </thead> 
        <tbody> 
         <tr> 
          <td>status</td> 
          <td><tt>OK</tt> or <tt>ERROR</tt><br>Indicates whether the request was successful</td> 
         </tr> 
         <tr> 
          <td>url</td> 
          <td>HTTP URL that was passed in the input</td> 
         </tr> 
         <tr> 
          <td>language</td> 
          <td>Detected language of the source text (text with fewer than 15 characters is assumed to be English)</td> 
         </tr> 
         <tr> 
          <td>publicationDate</td> 
          <td>Object containing the date in <tt>yyyymmddThhmmss</tt> format, and a confidence indicator (<tt>yes</tt> or <tt>no</tt>)</td> 
         </tr> 
        </tbody> 
       </table> 
      </div> 
      <div class="annotation-block--right"> 
       <p class="code-header">Example response</p> 
       <pre><code class="json">
{
  "status": "OK",
  "usage": "By accessing AlchemyAPI or using information generated by AlchemyAPI, you are agreeing to be bound by the AlchemyAPI Terms of Use: http://www.alchemyapi.com/company/terms.html",
  "url": "https://www.whitehouse.gov/the-press-office/2016/03/19/weekly-address-president-obamas-supreme-court-nomination",
  "totalTransactions": "1",
  "language": "english",
  "publicationDate": {
    "confident": "yes",
    "date": "20160319T000000"
  }
}
            </code></pre> 
      </div>

     <h2 id="relations">Relations</h2> 
     <div class="method-curl annotation-block--left relations inputToggles"> 
      <span class="inputToggle" onclick="toggleMethod('relations', 'alchemy-html', this)">HTML</span> 
      <span class="inputToggle inputSelect" onclick="toggleMethod('relations', 'alchemy-url', this)">URL</span> 
      <span class="inputToggle" onclick="toggleMethod('relations', 'alchemy-text', this)">Text</span> 
      <p class="relations alchemy-html">Extract Subject-Action-Object relations from an HTML document.</p> 
      <p class="relations alchemy-url">Extract Subject-Action-Object relations from a webpage.</p> 
      <p class="relations alchemy-text">Extract Subject-Action-Object relations from plain text.</p> 
     </div> 
     <p class="method-node method-java method-python"> Extract Subject-Action-Object relations from a webpage, HTML, or plain text. </p> 
     <p> Supported languages: English, Spanish </p> 
     <pre class="method-curl nohighlight"><code class="relations alchemy-html">POST /html/HTMLGetRelations</code><code class="relations alchemy-url">GET /url/URLGetRelations<br>POST /url/URLGetRelations</code><code class="relations alchemy-text">POST /text/TextGetRelations</code></pre> 
     <pre class="method-node"><code class="javascript">relations(parameters, callback)</code></pre> 
     <pre class="method-python"><code class="python">relations(parameter=value,...)</code></pre> 
     <h3 id="request_relations relations">Request</h3> 
     <!-- update the id to match the method name, but in lower case --> 
     <!-- parameters --> 
     <div class="method-curl"> 
      <div class="annotation-block relations alchemy-html"> 
       <div class="annotation-block--left"> 
        <!-- If there are no parameters in the call, remove the table and include this paragraph:
            <p>No arguments</p>
            --> 
        <table class="align-right-1 unwrap-1"> 
         <thead> 
          <tr> 
           <th>Parameter</th> 
           <th>Type</th> 
           <th>Description</th> 
          </tr> 
         </thead> 
         <tbody> 
          <tr> 
           <td>apikey</td> 
           <td>query</td> 
           <td>(<strong>Required</strong>) Your API key</td> 
          </tr> 
          <tr> 
           <td>html</td> 
           <td>query</td> 
           <td>(<strong>Required</strong>) HTML content (must be URL encoded)</td> 
          </tr> 
          <tr> 
           <td>maxRetrieve</td> 
           <td>query</td> 
           <td>Maximum number of relations to return (default = 50, maximum = 100)</td> 
          </tr> 
          <tr> 
           <td>outputMode</td> 
           <td>query</td> 
           <td><tt>json</tt> or <tt>xml</tt> (default)</td> 
          </tr> 
          <tr> 
           <td>jsonp</td> 
           <td>query</td> 
           <td>JSONP callback (requires <tt>outputMode</tt> to be set to json)</td> 
          </tr> 
          <tr> 
           <td>url</td> 
           <td>query</td> 
           <td>Input here will appear as the <tt>url</tt> value in the response.</td> 
          </tr> 
          <tr> 
           <td>keywords</td> 
           <td>query</td> 
           <td>Set this to 1 to identify keywords in detected relations<br><strong>This incurs an additional transaction charge</strong></td> 
          </tr> 
          <tr> 
           <td>entities</td> 
           <td>query</td> 
           <td>Set this to 1 to identify named entities in detected relations<br><strong>This incurs an additional transaction charge</strong></td> 
          </tr> 
          <tr> 
           <td>requireEntities</td> 
           <td>query</td> 
           <td>Set this to 1 to restrict results to relations that contain at least one named entity</td> 
          </tr> 
          <tr> 
           <td>coreference</td> 
           <td>query</td> 
           <td>Set this to 0 to treat coreferences as separate entities (coreferences are resolved into detected entities by default)</td> 
          </tr> 
          <tr> 
           <td>disambiguate</td> 
           <td>query</td> 
           <td>Set this to 0 to hide entity disambiguation information in the response</td> 
          </tr> 
          <tr> 
           <td>knowledgeGraph</td> 
           <td>query</td> 
           <td>Set this to 1 to include knowledge graph information in the results<br><strong>This incurs an additional transaction charge</strong></td> 
          </tr> 
          <tr> 
           <td>linkedData</td> 
           <td>query</td> 
           <td>Set this to 0 to hide <a href="#linked-data">Linked Data</a> content links in the response</td> 
          </tr> 
          <tr> 
           <td>sentiment</td> 
           <td>query</td> 
           <td>Set this to 1 to analyze the sentiment towards each result<br><strong>This incurs an additional transaction charge</strong> </td> 
          </tr> 
          <tr> 
           <td>sentimentExcludeEntities</td> 
           <td>query</td> 
           <td>Set this to 1 to exclude named entity text from sentiment analysis. For exapmle, do not analyze "New" in "New York"</td> 
          </tr> 
          <tr> 
           <td>showSourceText</td> 
           <td>query</td> 
           <td>Set this to 1 to include the source text in the response</td> 
          </tr> 
          <tr> 
           <td>cquery</td> 
           <td>query</td> 
           <td>A <a href="../../../doc/alchemylanguage/visual_constraints.html">visual constraints query</a> to apply to the web page. Required when <tt>sourceText</tt> is set to <tt>cquery</tt></td> 
          </tr> 
          <tr> 
           <td>xpath</td> 
           <td>query</td> 
           <td>An XPath query to apply to the web page. Required when <tt>sourceText</tt> is set to one of the XPath values</td> 
          </tr> 
          <tr> 
           <td>sourceText</td> 
           <td>query</td> 
           <td>How to obtain the source text from the webpage. Possible values:<br> 
            <table class="descriptionTable"> 
             <tbody>
              <tr> 
               <td><tt>cleaned_or_raw</tt> (default)</td> 
               <td>Removes website elements such as links, ads, etc. If cleaning fails, raw web page text is used</td> 
              </tr> 
              <tr>
               <td><tt>cleaned</tt></td> 
               <td>Removes website elements such as links, ads, etc.</td> 
              </tr>
              <tr> 
               <td><tt>raw</tt></td> 
               <td>Uses raw web page text with no cleaning</td> 
              </tr> 
              <tr> 
               <td><tt>cquery</tt></td> 
               <td>Uses the <a href="../../../doc/alchemylanguage/visual_constraints.html">visual constraints query</a> that you specify in the <tt>cquery</tt> parameter</td> 
              </tr> 
              <tr> 
               <td><tt>xpath</tt></td> 
               <td>Uses the XPath query that you specify in the <tt>xpath</tt> parameter</td> 
              </tr> 
              <tr> 
               <td><tt>xpath_or_raw</tt></td> 
               <td>Uses the results of an XPath query that you specify in the <tt>xpath</tt> parameter, falling back to plain text if the XPath query returns nothing</td> 
              </tr> 
              <tr> 
               <td><tt>cleaned_and_xpath</tt></td> 
               <td>Uses the results of an XPath query on cleaned web page text</td> 
              </tr> 
             </tbody>
            </table> </td> 
          </tr> 
         </tbody> 
        </table> 
       </div> 
       <!-- request curl --> 
       <div class="annotation-block--right"> 
        <p class="code-header">Example request</p> 
        <pre class="method-curl"><code class="lang-bash">
curl -X POST -d "maxRetrieve=1" -d "outputMode=json" --data-urlencode html@nomination.html -d "url=https://www.whitehouse.gov/the-press-office/2016/03/19/weekly-address-president-obamas-supreme-court-nomination" "https://gateway-a.watsonplatform.net/calls/html/HTMLGetRelations?apikey=%API_KEY%"
            </code></pre> 
       </div> 
      </div>

           <td>maxRetrieve</td> 
           <td>query</td> 
           <td>Maximum number of entities to return (default = 50, maximum = 100)</td> 
          </tr> 
          <tr> 
           <td>outputMode</td> 
           <td>query</td> 
           <td><tt>json</tt> or <tt>xml</tt> (default)</td> 
          </tr> 
          <tr> 
           <td>jsonp</td> 
           <td>query</td> 
           <td>JSONP callback (requires <tt>outputMode</tt> to be set to json)</td> 
          </tr> 
          <tr> 
           <td>url</td> 
           <td>query</td> 
           <td>Input here will appear as the <tt>url</tt> value in the response.</td> 
          </tr> 
          <tr> 
           <td>keywords</td> 
           <td>query</td> 
           <td>Set this to 1 to identify keywords in detected relations<br><strong>This incurs an additional transaction charge</strong></td> 
          </tr> 
          <tr> 
           <td>entities</td> 
           <td>query</td> 
           <td>Set this to 1 to identify named entities in detected relations<br><strong>This incurs an additional transaction charge</strong></td> 
          </tr> 
          <tr> 
           <td>requireEntities</td> 
           <td>query</td> 
           <td>Set this to 1 to restrict results to relations that contain at least one named entity</td> 
          </tr> 
          <tr> 
           <td>coreference</td> 
           <td>query</td> 
           <td>Set this to 0 to treat coreferences as separate entities (coreferences are resolved into detected entities by default)</td> 
          </tr> 
          <tr> 
           <td>disambiguate</td> 
           <td>query</td> 
           <td>Set this to 0 to hide entity disambiguation information in the response</td> 
          </tr> 
          <tr> 
           <td>knowledgeGraph</td> 
           <td>query</td> 
           <td>Set this to 1 to include knowledge graph information in the results<br><strong>This incurs an additional transaction charge</strong></td> 
          </tr> 
          <tr> 
           <td>linkedData</td> 
           <td>query</td> 
           <td>Set this to 0 to hide <a href="#linked-data">Linked Data</a> content links in the response</td> 
          </tr> 
          <tr> 
           <td>sentiment</td> 
           <td>query</td> 
           <td>Set this to 1 to analyze the sentiment towards each result<br><strong>This incurs an additional transaction charge</strong> </td> 
          </tr> 
          <tr> 
           <td>sentimentExcludeEntities</td> 
           <td>query</td> 
           <td>Set this to 1 to exclude named entity text from sentiment analysis. For exapmle, do not analyze "New" in "New York"</td> 
          </tr> 
          <tr> 
           <td>showSourceText</td> 
           <td>query</td> 
           <td>Set this to 1 to include the source text in the response</td> 
          </tr> 
         </tbody> 
        </table> 
       </div> 
       <!-- request curl --> 
       <div class="annotation-block--right">

curl -X POST -d "maxRetrieve=1" -d "outputMode=json" --data-urlencode text@nomination.txt -d "url=https://www.whitehouse.gov/the-press-office/2016/03/19/weekly-address-president-obamas-supreme-court-nomination" "https://gateway-a.watsonplatform.net/calls/text/TextGetRelations?apikey=%API_KEY%"
            </code></pre>
