            <table class="descriptionTable"> 
             <tbody>

               <td><tt>cleaned_or_raw</tt> (default)</td> 
               <td>Removes website elements such as links, ads, etc. If cleaning fails, raw web page text is used</td> 
              </tr> 
              <tr>
               <td><tt>cleaned</tt></td> 
               <td>Removes website elements such as links, ads, etc.</td> 
              </tr>
              <tr> 
               <td><tt>raw</tt></td> 
               <td>Uses raw web page text with no cleaning</td> 
              </tr> 
              <tr>

              </tr> 
              <tr> 
               <td><tt>xpath</tt></td> 
               <td>Uses the XPath query that you specify in the <tt>xpath</tt> parameter</td> 
              </tr> 
              <tr> 
               <td><tt>xpath_or_raw</tt></td> 
               <td>Uses the results of an XPath query that you specify in the <tt>xpath</tt> parameter, falling back to plain text if the XPath query returns nothing</td> 
              </tr> 
              <tr> 
               <td><tt>cleaned_and_xpath</tt></td> 
               <td>Uses the results of an XPath query on cleaned web page text</td> 
              </tr> 
             </tbody>
            </table> </td> 
          </tr> 
         </tbody>

};

  if (err)
    console.log('error:', err);

                 </tr>

                 </tr> 
                </tbody>
               </table> </td> 
             </tr>

                 </tr> 
                 <tr> 
                  <td>sentimentFromSubject</td> 
                  <td><a href="#sentiment">Sentiment Analysis</a> data targeted towards the object, from the subject, via the action. Set <tt>sentiment</tt> to <tt>1</tt> to enable this in the response</td> 
                 </tr>

     <h2 id="typed_relations">Typed Relations</h2> 
     <div class="method-curl annotation-block--left typed_relations inputToggles"> 
      <span class="inputToggle" onclick="toggleMethod('typed_relations', 'alchemy-html', this)">HTML</span> 
      <span class="inputToggle inputSelect" onclick="toggleMethod('typed_relations', 'alchemy-url', this)">URL</span> 
      <span class="inputToggle" onclick="toggleMethod('typed_relations', 'alchemy-text', this)">Text</span> 
      <p class="typed_relations alchemy-html">Use custom models to identify typed relations between detected entities in an HTML document.</p> 
      <p class="typed_relations alchemy-url">Use custom models to identify typed relations between detected entities from a webpage.</p> 
      <p class="typed_relations alchemy-text">Use custom models to identify typed relations between detected entities in plain text.</p> 
     </div> 
     <p class="method-node method-java method-python"> Use custom models to identify typed relations between detected entities from a webpage, HTML, or plain text. </p> 
     <p> Typed relations identify different types of connections between detected entities. For example, the entities "Oscar" and "Leonardo DiCaprio" might be linked by an "awardedTo" relation. To tailor results for your domain, you can specify your own custom entities and relations with <a href="../../../doc/alchemylanguage/customizing.html">custom models</a> in Watson Knowledge Studio. </p> 
     <p> <b>Note: </b> Source text in Typed Relations calls is truncated to 5 KB </p> 
     <pre class="method-curl nohighlight"><code class="typed_relations alchemy-html">POST /html/HTMLGetTypedRelations</code><code class="typed_relations alchemy-url">GET /url/URLGetTypedRelations<br>POST /url/URLGetTypedRelations</code><code class="typed_relations alchemy-text">POST /text/TextGetTypedRelations</code></pre> 
     <pre class="method-node"><code class="javascript">typedRelations(parameters, callback)</code></pre> 
     <pre class="method-python"><code class="python">typed_relations(parameter=value,...)</code></pre> 
     <h3 id="request_typed_relations">Request</h3> 
     <!-- update the id to match the method name, but in lower case --> 
     <!-- parameters --> 
     <div class="method-curl"> 
      <div class="typed_relations alchemy-url annotation-block">

          </tr>

           <td>query</td> 
           <td>The unique alphanumeric identifier for your custom model. You can also choose from the following public models: 
            <ul> 
             <li>en-news: trained on English news content (default)</li> 
             <li>es-news: trained on Spanish news content</li> 
             <li>ar-news: trained on Arabic news content</li> 
            </ul> </td> 
          </tr> 
          <tr> 
           <td>outputMode</td> 
           <td>query</td> 
           <td><tt>json</tt> or <tt>xml</tt> (default)</td>

          <tr> 
           <td>text</td> 
           <td>query</td> 
           <td>(<strong>Required</strong>) Text content (must be URL encoded)</td> 
          </tr> 
          <tr> 
           <td>model</td> 
           <td>query</td> 
           <td>The unique alphanumeric identifier for your custom model. You can also choose from the following public models: 
            <ul> 
             <li>en-news: trained on English news content (default)</li> 
             <li>es-news: trained on Spanish news content</li> 
             <li>ar-news: trained on Arabic news content</li> 
            </ul> </td> 
          </tr> 
          <tr> 
           <td>outputMode</td> 
           <td>query</td> 
           <td><tt>json</tt> or <tt>xml</tt> (default)</td> 
          </tr> 
          <tr> 
           <td>showSourceText</td> 
           <td>query</td> 
           <td>Set this to 1 to include the source text in the response</td> 
          </tr> 
          <tr> 
           <td>url</td> 
           <td>query</td> 
           <td>Input here will appear as the <tt>url</tt> value in the response</td> 
          </tr> 
          <tr> 
           <td>jsonp</td> 
           <td>query</td> 
           <td>Desired JSONP callback (requires <tt>outputMode</tt> to be set to <tt>json</tt>)</td> 
          </tr> 
         </tbody> 
        </table> 
       </div> 
       <div class="annotation-block--right"> 
        <p class="code-header">Example request</p> 
        <pre class="method-curl"><code class="lang-bash">
  curl -X POST -d "outputMode=json" --data-urlencode text@ibm_site.txt -d "url=http://techcrunch.com" "https://gateway-a.watsonplatform.net/calls/text/TextGetTypedRelations?apikey=%API_KEY%&amp;model=en-news"
              </code></pre> 
       </div>

     <h3 id="response_typed_relations">Response</h3> 
     <!-- update the id to match the method name, but in lower case -->

         </tr>

          <td>url</td> 
          <td>HTTP URL that was passed in the input</td> 
         </tr> 
         <tr> 
          <td>typedRelations</td> 
          <td>array of relation objects 
           <table class="descriptionTable"> 
            <tbody>
             <tr> 
              <td>arguments</td> 
              <td>Array of entities involved in the relation. Each entity is assigned a <tt>part</tt> in the relation, which indicates its position in the relation, and an <tt>id</tt>, a unique identifier for that entity. The entity type is also displayed.</td> 
             </tr> 
             <tr>
              <td>score</td> 
              <td>Confidence score between <tt>0.0</tt> and <tt>1.0</tt>. The higher the score, the greater the confidence</td> 
             </tr>
             <tr> 
              <td>sentence</td> 
              <td>Text from the document where the relation was detected</td> 
             </tr> 
             <tr> 
              <td>type</td> 
              <td>The type of relation detected between the entities</td> 
             </tr> 
            </tbody>
           </table> </td> 
         </tr> 
        </tbody>

     <h2 id="sentiment">Sentiment Analysis</h2> 
     <div class="method-curl annotation-block--left sentiment inputToggles"> 
      <span class="inputToggle" onclick="toggleMethod('sentiment', 'alchemy-html', this)">HTML</span> 
      <span class="inputToggle inputSelect" onclick="toggleMethod('sentiment', 'alchemy-url', this)">URL</span> 
      <span class="inputToggle" onclick="toggleMethod('sentiment', 'alchemy-text', this)">Text</span> 
      <p class="sentiment alchemy-html">Analyze the overall sentiment of an HTML document.</p> 
      <p class="sentiment alchemy-url">Analyze the overall sentiment of a webpage.</p> 
      <p class="sentiment alchemy-text">Analyze the overall sentiment of plain text.</p> 
     </div> 
     <p class="method-node method-java method-python"> Analyze the overall sentiment of a webpage, HTML, or plain text. </p> 
     <p> Supported languages: Arabic, English, French, German, Italian, Portuguese, Russian, Spanish </p> 
     <pre class="method-curl nohighlight"><code class="sentiment alchemy-html">POST /html/HTMLGetTextSentiment</code><code class="sentiment alchemy-url">GET /url/URLGetTextSentiment<br>POST /url/URLGetTextSentiment</code><code class="sentiment alchemy-text">POST /text/TextGetTextSentiment</code></pre> 
     <pre class="method-node"><code class="javascript">sentiment(parameters, callback)</code></pre> 
     <pre class="method-python"><code class="python">sentiment(parameter=value,...)</code></pre> 
     <h3 id="request_sentiment">Request</h3> 
     <!-- update the id to match the method name, but in lower case --> 
     <!-- parameters --> 
     <div class="method-curl"> 
      <div class="annotation-block sentiment alchemy-html"> 
       <div class="annotation-block--left"> 
        <!-- If there are no parameters in the call, remove the table and include this paragraph:
            <p>No arguments</p>
            --> 
        <table class="align-right-1 unwrap-1"> 
         <thead> 
          <tr> 
           <th>Parameter</th> 
           <th>Type</th> 
           <th>Description</th> 
          </tr> 
         </thead> 
         <tbody> 
          <tr> 
           <td>apikey</td> 
           <td>query</td> 
           <td>(<strong>Required</strong>) Your API key</td> 
          </tr> 
          <tr> 
           <td>html</td> 
           <td>query</td> 
           <td>(<strong>Required</strong>) HTML content (must be URL encoded)</td> 
          </tr> 
          <tr> 
           <td>outputMode</td> 
           <td>query</td> 
           <td><tt>json</tt> or <tt>xml</tt> (default)</td> 
          </tr> 
          <tr> 
           <td>jsonp</td> 
           <td>query</td> 
           <td>JSONP callback (requires <tt>outputMode</tt> to be set to json)</td> 
          </tr> 
          <tr> 
           <td>url</td> 
           <td>query</td> 
           <td>Input here will appear as the <tt>url</tt> value in the response.</td> 
          </tr> 
          <tr> 
           <td>showSourceText</td> 
           <td>query</td> 
           <td>Set this to 1 to include the source text in the response</td> 
          </tr> 
          <tr> 
           <td>cquery</td> 
           <td>query</td> 
           <td>A <a href="../../../doc/alchemylanguage/visual_constraints.html">visual constraints query</a> to apply to the web page. Required when <tt>sourceText</tt> is set to <tt>cquery</tt></td> 
          </tr> 
          <tr> 
           <td>xpath</td> 
           <td>query</td> 
           <td>An XPath query to apply to the web page. Required when <tt>sourceText</tt> is set to one of the XPath values</td> 
          </tr> 
          <tr> 
           <td>sourceText</td> 
           <td>query</td> 
           <td>How to obtain the source text from the webpage. Possible values: 
            <table class="descriptionTable"> 
             <tbody>
              <tr> 
               <td><tt>cleaned_or_raw</tt> (default)</td> 
               <td>Removes website elements such as links, ads, etc. If cleaning fails, raw web page text is used</td> 
              </tr> 
              <tr>
               <td><tt>cleaned</tt></td> 
               <td>Removes website elements such as links, ads, etc.</td> 
              </tr>
              <tr> 
               <td><tt>raw</tt></td> 
               <td>Uses raw web page text with no cleaning</td> 
              </tr> 
              <tr> 
               <td><tt>cquery</tt></td> 
               <td>Uses the <a href="../../../doc/alchemylanguage/visual_constraints.html">visual constraints query</a> that you specify in the <tt>cquery</tt> parameter</td> 
              </tr> 
              <tr> 
               <td><tt>xpath</tt></td> 
               <td>Uses the XPath query that you specify in the <tt>xpath</tt> parameter</td> 
              </tr> 
              <tr> 
               <td><tt>xpath_or_raw</tt></td> 
               <td>Uses the results of an XPath query that you specify in the <tt>xpath</tt> parameter, falling back to plain text if the XPath query returns nothing</td> 
              </tr> 
              <tr> 
               <td><tt>cleaned_and_xpath</tt></td> 
               <td>Uses the results of an XPath query on cleaned web page text</td> 
              </tr> 
             </tbody>
            </table> </td> 
          </tr> 
         </tbody> 
        </table> 
       </div>

import json
from watson_developer_cloud import AlchemyLanguageV1

alchemy_language = AlchemyLanguageV1(api_key='API_KEY')
print(json.dumps(
  alchemy_language.sentiment(
    url='http://www.huffingtonpost.com/2010/06/22/iphone-4-review-the-worst_n_620714.html'),
  indent=2))
</code></pre>

     <h3 id="response_sentiment">Response</h3> 
     <!-- update the id to match the method name, but in lower case --> 
     <div class="annotation-block"> 
      <div class="annotation-block--left"> 
       <table class="align-right-1 unwrap-1"> 
        <thead> 
         <tr> 
          <th>Name</th> 
          <th>Description</th> 
         </tr> 
        </thead> 
        <tbody> 
         <tr> 
          <td>status</td> 
          <td><tt>OK</tt> or <tt>ERROR</tt><br>Indicates whether the request was successful</td> 
         </tr> 
         <tr> 
          <td>url</td> 
          <td>HTTP URL that was passed in the input</td> 
         </tr> 
         <tr> 
          <td>language</td> 
          <td>Detected language of the source text (text with fewer than 15 characters is assumed to be English)</td> 
         </tr> 
         <tr> 
          <td>docSentiment</td> 
          <td>Object containing document-level sentiment information 
           <table class="descriptionTable"> 
            <tbody>
             <tr> 
              <td>mixed</td> 
              <td><tt>1</tt> indicates that the sentiment is both positive and negative</td> 
             </tr> 
             <tr> 
              <td>score</td> 
              <td>Sentiment strength (<tt>0.0</tt> == neutral)</td> 
             </tr> 
             <tr> 
              <td>type</td> 
              <td>Sentiment polarity: <tt>positive</tt>, <tt>negative</tt>, or <tt>neutral</tt></td> 
             </tr> 
            </tbody>
           </table> </td> 
         </tr> 
        </tbody> 
       </table> 
      </div> 
      <div class="annotation-block--right"> 
       <p class="code-header">Example response</p> 
       <pre><code class="json">
{
  "status": "OK",
  "usage": "By accessing AlchemyAPI or using information generated by AlchemyAPI, you are agreeing to be bound by the AlchemyAPI Terms of Use: http://www.alchemyapi.com/company/terms.html",
  "url": "http://www.huffingtonpost.com/2010/06/22/iphone-4-review-the-worst_n_620714.html",
  "totalTransactions": "1",
  "language": "english",
  "docSentiment": {
    "mixed": "1",
    "score": "-0.24582",
    "type": "negative"
  }
}
            </code></pre> 
      </div>

     <h2 id="targeted_sentiment">Targeted Sentiment</h2> 
     <div class="method-curl annotation-block--left targeted_sentiment inputToggles"> 
      <span class="inputToggle" onclick="toggleMethod('targeted_sentiment', 'alchemy-html', this)">HTML</span> 
      <span class="inputToggle inputSelect" onclick="toggleMethod('targeted_sentiment', 'alchemy-url', this)">URL</span> 
      <span class="inputToggle" onclick="toggleMethod('targeted_sentiment', 'alchemy-text', this)">Text</span> 
      <p class="targeted_sentiment alchemy-html">Analyze sentiment for targeted phrases in an HTML document.</p> 
      <p class="targeted_sentiment alchemy-url">Analyze sentiment for targeted phrases on a webpage.</p> 
      <p class="targeted_sentiment alchemy-text">Analyze sentiment for targeted phrases in plain text.</p> 
     </div> 
     <p class="method-node method-java method-python"> Analyze sentiment for targeted phrases in a webpage, HTML, or plain text. </p> 
     <p> Supported languages: Arabic, English, French, German, Italian, Portuguese, Russian, Spanish </p> 
     <pre class="method-curl nohighlight"><code class="targeted_sentiment alchemy-html">POST /html/HTMLGetTargetedSentiment</code><code class="targeted_sentiment alchemy-url">GET /url/URLGetTargetedSentiment<br>POST /url/URLGetTargetedSentiment</code><code class="targeted_sentiment alchemy-text">POST /text/TextGetTargetedSentiment</code></pre> 
     <pre class="method-node"><code class="javascript">sentiment(parameters, callback)</code></pre> 
     <pre class="method-python"><code class="javascript">targeted_sentiment(parameter=value,...)</code></pre> 
     <h3 id="request_targeted_sentiment targeted_sentiment">Request</h3> 
     <!-- update the id to match the method name, but in lower case --> 
     <!-- parameters --> 
     <div class="method-curl"> 
      <div class="annotation-block targeted_sentiment alchemy-html"> 
       <div class="annotation-block--left"> 
        <!-- If there are no parameters in the call, remove the table and include this paragraph:
            <p>No arguments</p>
            --> 
        <table class="align-right-1 unwrap-1"> 
         <thead> 
          <tr> 
           <th>Parameter</th> 
           <th>Type</th> 
           <th>Description</th> 
          </tr> 
         </thead> 
         <tbody> 
          <tr> 
           <td>apikey</td> 
           <td>query</td> 
           <td>(<strong>Required</strong>) Your API key</td> 
          </tr> 
          <tr> 
           <td>html</td> 
           <td>query</td> 
           <td>(<strong>Required</strong>) HTML content (must be URL encoded)</td> 
          </tr> 
          <tr> 
           <td>targets</td> 
           <td>query</td> 
           <td>(<strong>Required</strong>) <tt>phrase1|phrase2|...</tt><br>Pipe delimited list of phrases. The service will return sentiment information for each phrase that is found in the source text. Supports up to 20 phrases.</td> 
          </tr> 
          <tr> 
           <td>outputMode</td> 
           <td>query</td> 
           <td><tt>json</tt> or <tt>xml</tt> (default)</td> 
          </tr> 
          <tr> 
           <td>jsonp</td> 
           <td>query</td> 
           <td>JSONP callback (requires <tt>outputMode</tt> to be set to json)</td> 
          </tr> 
          <tr> 
           <td>url</td> 
           <td>query</td> 
           <td>Input here will appear as the <tt>url</tt> value in the response.</td> 
          </tr> 
          <tr>
           <td>showSourceText</td> 
           <td>query</td> 
           <td>Set this to 1 to include the source text in the response</td> 
          </tr> 
          <tr> 
           <td>cquery</td> 
           <td>query</td> 
           <td>A <a href="../../../doc/alchemylanguage/visual_constraints.html">visual constraints query</a> to apply to the web page. Required when <tt>sourceText</tt> is set to <tt>cquery</tt></td> 
          </tr> 
          <tr> 
           <td>xpath</td> 
           <td>query</td> 
           <td>An XPath query to apply to the web page. Required when <tt>sourceText</tt> is set to one of the XPath values</td> 
          </tr> 
          <tr> 
           <td>sourceText</td> 
           <td>query</td> 
           <td>How to obtain the source text from the webpage. Possible values:<br> 
            <table class="descriptionTable"> 
             <tbody>
              <tr> 
               <td><tt>cleaned_or_raw</tt> (default)</td> 
               <td>Removes website elements such as links, ads, etc. If cleaning fails, raw web page text is used</td> 
              </tr> 
              <tr>
               <td><tt>cleaned</tt></td> 
               <td>Removes website elements such as links, ads, etc.</td> 
              </tr>
              <tr> 
               <td><tt>raw</tt></td> 
               <td>Uses raw web page text with no cleaning</td> 
              </tr> 
              <tr> 
               <td><tt>cquery</tt></td> 
               <td>Uses the <a href="../../../doc/alchemylanguage/visual_constraints.html">visual constraints query</a> that you specify in the <tt>cquery</tt> parameter</td> 
              </tr> 
              <tr> 
               <td><tt>xpath</tt></td> 
               <td>Uses the XPath query that you specify in the <tt>xpath</tt> parameter</td> 
              </tr> 
              <tr> 
               <td><tt>xpath_or_raw</tt></td> 
               <td>Uses the results of an XPath query that you specify in the <tt>xpath</tt> parameter, falling back to plain text if the XPath query returns nothing</td> 
              </tr> 
              <tr> 
               <td><tt>cleaned_and_xpath</tt></td> 
               <td>Uses the results of an XPath query on cleaned web page text</td> 
              </tr> 
             </tbody>
            </table> </td> 
          </tr> 
         </tbody> 
        </table> 
       </div> 
       <!-- request curl --> 
       <div class="annotation-block--right"> 
        <p class="code-header">Example request</p> 
        <pre class="method-curl"><code class="lang-bash">
curl -X POST -d "outputMode=json" -d "targets=NASDAQ|Dow" --data-urlencode html@stock_market_news.html -d "url=http://www.zacks.com/stock/news/207968/stock-market-news-for-february-19-2016" "https://gateway-a.watsonplatform.net/calls/html/HTMLGetTargetedSentiment?apikey=%API_KEY%"
            </code></pre> 
       </div> 
      </div>

var watson = require('watson-developer-cloud');
var alchemy_language = watson.alchemy_language({
  api_key: 'API_KEY'
})

var parameters = {
  url: 'http://www.zacks.com/stock/news/207968/stock-market-news-for-february-19-2016',
  targets: [
    'NASDAQ',
    'Dow'
  ]
};

alchemy_language.sentiment(parameters, function (err, response) {
  if (err)
    console.log('error:', err);
  else
    console.log(JSON.stringify(response, null, 2));
});</code></pre>

     <h3 id="response_targeted_sentiment">Response</h3> 
     <!-- update the id to match the method name, but in lower case --> 
     <div class="annotation-block"> 
      <div class="annotation-block--left"> 
       <table class="align-right-1 unwrap-1"> 
        <thead> 
         <tr> 
          <th>Name</th> 
          <th>Description</th> 
         </tr> 
        </thead> 
        <tbody> 
         <tr> 
          <td>status</td> 
          <td><tt>OK</tt> or <tt>ERROR</tt><br>Indicates whether the request was successful</td> 
         </tr> 
         <tr> 
          <td>url</td> 
          <td>HTTP URL that was passed in the input</td> 
         </tr> 
         <tr> 
          <td>language</td> 
          <td>Detected language of the source text (text with fewer than 15 characters is assumed to be English)</td> 
         </tr> 
         <tr> 
          <td>results</td> 
          <td>Array of sentiment result objects 
           <table class="descriptionTable"> 
            <tbody>
             <tr> 
              <td>mixed</td> 
              <td><tt>1</tt> indicates that the sentiment is both positive and negative</td> 
             </tr> 
             <tr> 
              <td>score</td> 
              <td>Sentiment strength (<tt>0.0</tt> == neutral)</td> 
             </tr> 
             <tr> 
              <td>type</td> 
              <td>Sentiment polarity: <tt>positive</tt>, <tt>negative</tt>, or <tt>neutral</tt></td> 
             </tr> 
             <tr> 
              <td>text</td> 
              <td>The targeted phrase associated with the sentiment information</td> 
             </tr> 
            </tbody>
           </table> </td> 
         </tr> 
         <tr> 
          <td>statusInfo</td> 
          <td>In addition to the generic <a href="#error-handling">error messages</a>, this can contain <tt>cannot-locate-keyphrase</tt> when the sentiment target is not found in the text.</td> 
         </tr> 
        </tbody> 
       </table> 
      </div> 
      <div class="annotation-block--right"> 
       <p class="code-header">Example response</p> 
       <pre><code class="json">
{
  "status": "OK",
  "usage": "By accessing AlchemyAPI or using information generated by AlchemyAPI, you are agreeing to be bound by the AlchemyAPI Terms of Use: http://www.alchemyapi.com/company/terms.html",
  "url": "http://www.zacks.com/stock/news/207968/stock-market-news-for-february-19-2016",
  "totalTransactions": "1",
  "language": "english",
  "results": [
    {
      "sentiment": {
        "score": "-0.387744",
        "type": "negative"
      },
      "text": "NASDAQ"
    },
    {
      "sentiment": {
        "score": "-0.416076",
        "type": "negative"
      },
      "text": "Dow"
    }
  ]
}
            </code></pre> 
      </div> 
     </div> 
     <!-- method: end --> 
     <!-- method: begin --> 
     <h2 id="taxonomy">Taxonomy</h2> 
     <div class="method-curl annotation-block--left taxonomy inputToggles"> 
      <span class="inputToggle" onclick="toggleMethod('taxonomy', 'alchemy-html', this)">HTML</span> 
      <span class="inputToggle inputSelect" onclick="toggleMethod('taxonomy', 'alchemy-url', this)">URL</span> 
      <span class="inputToggle" onclick="toggleMethod('taxonomy', 'alchemy-text', this)">Text</span> 
      <p class="taxonomy alchemy-html">Categorize an HTML document into a 5-level taxonomy.</p> 
      <p class="taxonomy alchemy-url">Categorize a webpage into a 5-level taxonomy.</p> 
      <p class="taxonomy alchemy-text">Categorize plain text into a 5-level taxonomy.</p> 
     </div> 
     <p class="method-node method-java method-python"> Categorize a webpage, HTML, or plain text into a 5-level taxonomy. </p> 
     <p>Download the complete list of taxonomy categories: <a href="https://github.com/watson-developer-cloud/doc-tutorial-downloads/raw/master/alchemy-language/taxonomy-hierarchy.pdf">PDF</a> | <a download="taxonomy-hierarchy.xlsx" href="https://github.com/watson-developer-cloud/doc-tutorial-downloads/blob/master/alchemy-language/taxonomy-hierarchy.xlsx?raw=true">XLSX</a> | <a download="taxonomy-hierarchy.csv" href="https://github.com/watson-developer-cloud/doc-tutorial-downloads/blob/master/alchemy-language/taxonomy-hierarchy.csv">CSV</a></p> 
     <p> Supported languages: English </p> 
     <pre class="method-curl nohighlight"><code class="taxonomy alchemy-html">POST /html/HTMLGetRankedTaxonomy</code><code class="taxonomy alchemy-url">GET /url/URLGetRankedTaxonomy<br>POST /url/URLGetRankedTaxonomy</code><code class="taxonomy alchemy-text">POST /text/TextGetRankedTaxonomy</code></pre> 
     <pre class="method-node"><code class="javascript">taxonomy(parameters, callback)</code></pre> 
     <pre class="method-python"><code class="python">taxonomy(parameter=value,...)</code></pre> 
     <h3 id="request_taxonomy taxonomy">Request</h3> 
     <!-- update the id to match the method name, but in lower case --> 
     <!-- parameters --> 
     <div class="method-curl"> 
      <div class="annotation-block taxonomy alchemy-html"> 
       <div class="annotation-block--left"> 
        <!-- If there are no parameters in the call, remove the table and include this paragraph:
            <p>No arguments</p>
            --> 
        <table class="align-right-1 unwrap-1"> 
         <thead> 
          <tr> 
           <th>Parameter</th> 
           <th>Type</th> 
           <th>Description</th> 
          </tr> 
         </thead> 
         <tbody> 
          <tr> 
           <td>apikey</td> 
           <td>query</td> 
           <td>(<strong>Required</strong>) Your API key</td> 
          </tr> 
          <tr> 
           <td>html</td> 
           <td>query</td> 
           <td>(<strong>Required</strong>) HTML content (must be URL encoded)</td> 
          </tr> 
          <tr> 
           <td>outputMode</td> 
           <td>query</td> 
           <td><tt>json</tt> or <tt>xml</tt> (default)</td> 
          </tr> 
          <tr> 
           <td>jsonp</td> 
           <td>query</td> 
           <td>JSONP callback (requires <tt>outputMode</tt> to be set to json)</td> 
          </tr> 
          <tr> 
           <td>url</td> 
           <td>query</td> 
           <td>Input here will appear as the <tt>url</tt> value in the response.</td> 
          </tr> 
          <tr> 
           <td>showSourceText</td> 
           <td>query</td> 
           <td>Set this to 1 to include the source text in the response</td> 
          </tr> 
          <tr> 
           <td>cquery</td> 
           <td>query</td> 
           <td>A <a href="../../../doc/alchemylanguage/visual_constraints.html">visual constraints query</a> to apply to the web page. Required when <tt>sourceText</tt> is set to <tt>cquery</tt></td> 
          </tr> 
          <tr> 
           <td>xpath</td> 
           <td>query</td> 
           <td>An XPath query to apply to the web page. Required when <tt>sourceText</tt> is set to one of the XPath values</td> 
          </tr> 
          <tr> 
           <td>sourceText</td> 
           <td>query</td> 
           <td>How to obtain the source text from the webpage. Possible values:<br> 
            <table class="descriptionTable"> 
             <tbody>
              <tr> 
               <td><tt>cleaned_or_raw</tt> (default)</td> 
               <td>Removes website elements such as links, ads, etc. If cleaning fails, raw web page text is used</td> 
              </tr> 
              <tr>
               <td><tt>cleaned</tt></td> 
               <td>Removes website elements such as links, ads, etc.</td> 
              </tr>
              <tr> 
               <td><tt>raw</tt></td> 
               <td>Uses raw web page text with no cleaning</td> 
              </tr> 
              <tr> 
               <td><tt>cquery</tt></td> 
               <td>Uses the <a href="../../../doc/alchemylanguage/visual_constraints.html">visual constraints query</a> that you specify in the <tt>cquery</tt> parameter</td> 
              </tr> 
              <tr> 
               <td><tt>xpath</tt></td> 
               <td>Uses the XPath query that you specify in the <tt>xpath</tt> parameter</td> 
              </tr> 
              <tr> 
               <td><tt>xpath_or_raw</tt></td> 
               <td>Uses the results of an XPath query that you specify in the <tt>xpath</tt> parameter, falling back to plain text if the XPath query returns nothing</td> 
              </tr> 
              <tr> 
               <td><tt>cleaned_and_xpath</tt></td> 
               <td>Uses the results of an XPath query on cleaned web page text</td> 
              </tr> 
             </tbody>
            </table> </td> 
          </tr> 
         </tbody> 
        </table> 
       </div>

        <pre><code class="python">
import json
from watson_developer_cloud import AlchemyLanguageV1

alchemy_language = AlchemyLanguageV1(api_key='API_KEY')
print(json.dumps(
  alchemy_language.taxonomy(
    url='cnn.com'),
  indent=2))

     <h3 id="response_taxonomy">Response</h3> 
     <!-- update the id to match the method name, but in lower case --> 
     <div class="annotation-block"> 
      <div class="annotation-block--left"> 
       <table class="align-right-1 unwrap-1"> 
        <thead> 
         <tr> 
          <th>Name</th> 
          <th>Description</th> 
         </tr> 
        </thead> 
        <tbody> 
         <tr> 
          <td>status</td> 
          <td><tt>OK</tt> or <tt>ERROR</tt><br>Indicates whether the request was successful</td> 
         </tr> 
         <tr> 
          <td>url</td> 
          <td>HTTP URL that was passed in the input</td> 
         </tr> 
         <tr> 
          <td>language</td> 
          <td>Detected language of the source text (text with fewer than 15 characters is assumed to be English)</td> 
         </tr> 
         <tr> 
          <td>taxonomy</td> 
          <td>Array of objects containing information about the detected categories 
           <table class="descriptionTable"> 
            <tbody>
             <tr> 
              <td>label</td> 
              <td>Detected category</td> 
             </tr> 
             <tr> 
              <td>score</td> 
              <td>Confidence score between <tt>0.0</tt> and <tt>1.0</tt>. The higher the score, the greater the confidence</td> 
             </tr> 
            </tbody>
           </table> </td> 
         </tr> 
        </tbody> 
       </table> 
      </div> 
      <div class="annotation-block--right">

  "url": "http://www.cnn.com/",
  "totalTransactions": "1",
  "language": "english",
  "taxonomy": [
    {
      "label": "/news",
      "score": "0.994385"

     <h2 id="text_cleaned">Text (cleaned)</h2> 
     <div class="method-curl annotation-block--left text_cleaned inputToggles"> 
      <span class="inputToggle" onclick="toggleMethod('text_cleaned', 'alchemy-html', this)">HTML</span> 
      <span class="inputToggle inputSelect" onclick="toggleMethod('text_cleaned', 'alchemy-url', this)">URL</span> 
      <p class="text_cleaned alchemy-html">Extract primary text content from an HTML document.</p> 
      <p class="text_cleaned alchemy-url">Extract primary text content from a webpage.</p> 
     </div> 
     <p class="method-node method-java method-python"> Extract primary text content from a webpage or HTML. </p> 
     <p> Cleaned page text is obtained by default in other HTML and URL functions. You can view the results of page cleaning in responses from most of the other methods by passing <tt>showSourceText=1</tt>. </p> 
     <pre class="method-curl nohighlight"><code class="text_cleaned alchemy-html">POST /html/HTMLGetText</code><code class="text_cleaned alchemy-url">GET /url/URLGetText<br>POST /url/URLGetText</code></pre> 
     <pre class="method-node"><code class="javascript">text(parameters, callback)</code></pre> 
     <pre class="method-python"><code class="python">text(parameter=value,...)</code></pre> 
     <h3 id="request_text_cleaned text_cleaned">Request</h3> 
     <!-- update the id to match the method name, but in lower case --> 
     <!-- parameters --> 
     <div class="method-curl"> 
      <div class="annotation-block text_cleaned alchemy-html"> 
       <div class="annotation-block--left"> 
        <!-- If there are no parameters in the call, remove the table and include this paragraph:
            <p>No arguments</p>
            --> 
        <table class="align-right-1 unwrap-1"> 
         <thead> 
          <tr> 
           <th>Parameter</th> 
           <th>Type</th> 
           <th>Description</th> 
          </tr> 
         </thead> 
         <tbody> 
          <tr> 
           <td>apikey</td> 
           <td>query</td> 
           <td>(<strong>Required</strong>) Your API key</td> 
          </tr> 
          <tr> 
           <td>html</td> 
           <td>query</td> 
           <td>(<strong>Required</strong>) HTML content (must be URL encoded)</td> 
          </tr> 
          <tr> 
           <td>extractLinks</td> 
           <td>query</td> 
           <td>Set this to 1 to include hyperlinks in the extracted text</td> 
          </tr> 
          <tr> 
           <td>useMetadata</td> 
           <td>query</td> 
           <td>Set this to 0 to ignore description information in webpage metadata</td> 
          </tr> 
          <tr> 
           <td>outputMode</td> 
           <td>query</td> 
           <td><tt>json</tt> or <tt>xml</tt> (default)</td> 
          </tr> 
          <tr> 
           <td>jsonp</td> 
           <td>query</td> 
           <td>JSONP callback (requires <tt>outputMode</tt> to be set to json)</td> 
          </tr> 
          <tr> 
           <td>url</td> 
           <td>query</td> 
           <td>Input here will appear as the <tt>url</tt> value in the response.</td> 
          </tr> 
          <tr> 
           <td>cquery</td> 
           <td>query</td> 
           <td>A <a href="../../../doc/alchemylanguage/visual_constraints.html">visual constraints query</a> to apply to the web page. Required when <tt>sourceText</tt> is set to <tt>cquery</tt></td> 
          </tr> 
          <tr> 
           <td>xpath</td> 
           <td>query</td> 
           <td>An XPath query to apply to the web page. Required when <tt>sourceText</tt> is set to one of the XPath values</td> 
          </tr> 
          <tr> 
           <td>sourceText</td> 
           <td>query</td> 
           <td>How to obtain the source text from the webpage. Possible values:<br> 
            <table class="descriptionTable"> 
             <tbody>
              <tr> 
               <td><tt>cleaned_or_raw</tt> (default)</td> 
               <td>Removes website elements such as links, ads, etc. If cleaning fails, raw web page text is used</td> 
              </tr> 
              <tr>
               <td><tt>cleaned</tt></td> 
               <td>Removes website elements such as links, ads, etc.</td> 
              </tr>
              <tr> 
               <td><tt>raw</tt></td> 
               <td>Uses raw web page text with no cleaning</td> 
              </tr> 
              <tr> 
               <td><tt>cquery</tt></td> 
               <td>Uses the <a href="../../../doc/alchemylanguage/visual_constraints.html">visual constraints query</a> that you specify in the <tt>cquery</tt> parameter</td> 
              </tr> 
              <tr> 
               <td><tt>xpath</tt></td> 
               <td>Uses the XPath query that you specify in the <tt>xpath</tt> parameter</td> 
              </tr> 
              <tr> 
               <td><tt>xpath_or_raw</tt></td> 
               <td>Uses the results of an XPath query that you specify in the <tt>xpath</tt> parameter, falling back to plain text if the XPath query returns nothing</td> 
              </tr> 
              <tr> 
               <td><tt>cleaned_and_xpath</tt></td> 
               <td>Uses the results of an XPath query on cleaned web page text</td> 
              </tr> 
             </tbody>
            </table> </td> 
          </tr> 
         </tbody> 
        </table> 
       </div>

     <h3 id="response_text_cleaned">Response</h3>

          <th>Name</th> 
          <th>Description</th> 
         </tr> 
        </thead> 
        <tbody> 
         <tr> 
          <td>status</td>

         </tr> 
         <tr> 
          <td>url</td> 
          <td>HTTP URL that was passed in the input</td> 
         </tr> 
         <tr> 
          <td>language</td> 
          <td>Detected language of the source text (text with fewer than 15 characters is assumed to be English)</td> 
         </tr> 
         <tr> 
          <td>text</td> 
          <td>The extracted text</td>

     <h2 id="text_raw">Text (raw)</h2>

     </div>

     <pre class="method-curl nohighlight"><code class="text_raw alchemy-html">POST /html/HTMLGetRawText</code><code class="text_raw alchemy-url">GET /url/URLGetRawText<br>POST /url/URLGetRawText</code></pre>

})

var parameters = {
  url: 'http://techcrunch.com/2016/01/29/ibm-watson-weather-company-sale',
  raw: true
};

alchemy_language.text(parameters, function (err, response) {
  if (err)
    console.log('error:', err);
  else
    console.log(JSON.stringify(response, null, 2));
});</code></pre> 
       </div> 
      </div> 
     </div>

     <h2 id="title_extraction">Title Extraction</h2> 
     <div class="method-curl annotation-block--left title_extraction inputToggles"> 
      <span class="inputToggle" onclick="toggleMethod('title_extraction', 'alchemy-html', this)">HTML</span> 
      <span class="inputToggle inputSelect" onclick="toggleMethod('title_extraction', 'alchemy-url', this)">URL</span> 
      <p class="title_extraction alchemy-html">Extract the page title from an HTML document.</p> 
      <p class="title_extraction alchemy-url">Extract the page title from a webpage.</p> 
     </div> 
     <p class="method-node method-java method-python"> Extract the page title from a webpage or HTML. </p> 
     <pre class="method-curl nohighlight"><code class="title_extraction alchemy-html">POST /html/HTMLGetTitle</code><code class="title_extraction alchemy-url">GET /url/URLGetTitle<br>POST /url/URLGetTitle</code></pre> 
     <pre class="method-node"><code class="javascript">title(parameters, callback)</code></pre> 
     <pre class="method-python"><code class="python">title(parameter=value,...)</code></pre> 
     <h3 id="request_title_extraction title_extraction">Request</h3> 
     <!-- update the id to match the method name, but in lower case --> 
     <!-- parameters -->

       <div class="annotation-block--left">

     <h1 id="custom-models">Custom models</h1> 
     <p> The following methods allow you to manage custom models that are deployed to your AlchemyAPI service instance. With an <a target="_blank" href="https://console.ng.bluemix.net/catalog/services/alchemyapi">Advanced pricing plan</a> and access to <a href="http://ibm.biz/ibmwatsonknowledgestudio">Watson Knowledge Studio</a>, you can create your own custom model that specializes in understanding entities and relations that are unique to your domain. </p> 
     <p> Learn more about custom models and how to get started <a href="../../../doc/alchemylanguage/customizing.html">here.</a> </p> 
     <!-- method: begin --> 
     <h2 id="list-models">List models</h2> 
     <p> Lists the models available for your AlchemyAPI service instance. The list includes custom models that have been deployed from Watson Knowledge Studio as well as some default models that are available to all AlchemyLanguage users. </p> 
     <pre class="nohighlight"><code>GET /info/models</code></pre> 
     <h3>Request</h3> 
     <div class="annotation-block"> 
      <div class="annotation-block--left"> 
       <table class="align-right-1 unwrap-1 unwrap-2"> 
        <thead> 
         <tr> 
          <th>Parameter</th> 
          <th>Type</th> 
          <th>Description</th> 
         </tr> 
        </thead> 
        <tbody> 
         <tr> 
          <td>apikey</td> 
          <td>query</td> 
          <td>(<strong>Required</strong>) Your API key</td> 
         </tr> 
         <tr> 
          <td>outputMode</td> 
          <td>query</td> 
          <td><tt>json</tt> or <tt>xml</tt> (default)</td> 
         </tr> 
        </tbody> 
       </table> 
      </div> 
      <div class="annotation-block--right"> 
       <p class="code-header">Example request</p> 
       <pre class=""><code class="lang-bash">
curl -X GET -d "outputMode=json" "https://gateway-a.watsonplatform.net/calls/info/models?apikey=%API_KEY%"
            </code></pre> 
      </div> 
     </div> 
     <h3>Response</h3> 
     <div class="annotation-block"> 
      <div class="annotation-block--left"> 
       <table class="align-right-1 unwrap-1"> 
        <thead> 
         <tr> 
          <th>Name</th> 
          <th>Description</th> 
         </tr> 
        </thead> 
        <tbody> 
         <tr> 
          <td>status</td> 
          <td><tt>OK</tt> or <tt>ERROR</tt><br>Indicates whether the request was successful</td> 
         </tr> 
         <tr> 
          <td>models</td> 
          <td>Array of available models 
           <table class="descriptionTable"> 
            <tbody>
             <tr> 
              <td>status</td> 
              <td>The status of the model</td> 
             </tr> 
             <tr> 
              <td>model_id</td> 
              <td>The unique model identifier. Use this in supported API calls to override AlchemyLanguage's default model.</td> 
             </tr> 
             <tr> 
              <td>language</td> 
              <td>The language that is compatible with the model</td> 
             </tr> 
            </tbody>
           </table> </td> 
         </tr> 
        </tbody> 
       </table> 
      </div> 
      <div class="annotation-block--right"> 
       <p class="code-header">Example response</p> 
       <pre><code class="json">
{
  "status": "OK",
  "models": [
    {
      "status": "available",
      "model_id": "en-news",
      "language": "en",
      "description": "English relationship extraction"
    },
    {
      "status": "available",
      "model_id": "MODEL_KEY",
      "language": "en",
      "description": "My custom model deployed from Watson Knowledge Studio"
    }
  ]
}</code></pre> 
      </div> 
     </div> 
     <!-- method: end --> 
     <!-- method: begin --> 
     <h2 id="delete-model">Delete model</h2> 
     <p> Deletes a custom model that was deployed to your AlchemyAPI service instance from Watson Knowledge Studio. </p> 
     <pre class=" nohighlight"><code>DELETE /info/model/{model_id}</code></pre> 
     <h3>Request</h3> 
     <div class="annotation-block"> 
      <div class="annotation-block--left"> 
       <table class="align-right-1 unwrap-1 unwrap-2"> 
        <thead> 
         <tr> 
          <th>Parameter</th> 
          <th>Type</th> 
          <th>Description</th> 
         </tr> 
        </thead> 
        <tbody> 
         <tr> 
          <td>apikey</td> 
          <td>query</td> 
          <td>(<strong>Required</strong>) Your API key</td> 
         </tr> 
         <tr> 
          <td>model_id</td> 
          <td>path</td> 
          <td>The unique identifier for the model that you want to delete</td> 
         </tr> 
         <tr> 
          <td>outputMode</td> 
          <td>query</td> 
          <td><tt>json</tt> or <tt>xml</tt> (default)</td> 
         </tr> 
        </tbody> 
       </table> 
      </div> 
      <div class="annotation-block--right"> 
       <p class="code-header">Example request</p> 
       <pre class=""><code class="lang-bash">
curl -X DELETE -d "outputMode=json" "https://gateway-a.watsonplatform.net/calls/info/model/MODEL_ID?apikey=%API_KEY%"
            </code></pre> 
      </div> 
     </div> 
     <h3>Response</h3> 
     <div class="annotation-block"> 
      <div class="annotation-block--left"> 
       <table class="align-right-1 unwrap-1"> 
        <thead> 
         <tr> 
          <th>Name</th> 
          <th>Description</th> 
         </tr> 
        </thead> 
        <tbody> 
         <tr> 
          <td>status</td> 
          <td><tt>OK</tt> or <tt>ERROR</tt><br>Indicates whether the request was successful</td> 
         </tr> 
         <tr> 
          <td>statusInfo</td> 
          <td>Additional status information. In addition to the general error messages, this can contain: 
           <ul> 
            <li>model-deleted:MODEL_ID</li> 
            <li>model-does-not-exist:MODEL_ID</li> 
           </ul> </td> 
         </tr> 
        </tbody> 
       </table> 
      </div> 
      <div class="annotation-block--right"> 
       <p class="code-header">Example response</p> 
       <pre><code class="json">
{
  "status": "OK",
  "statusInfo": "model-deleted:MODEL_ID"
}
</code></pre> 
      </div> 
     </div> 
     <!-- method: end --> 
     <h1 id="data-collection">Data collection</h1> 
     <p> By default, all Watson services log requests and their results. Logging is done only to improve the services for future users. The logged data is not shared or made public. To prevent IBM from accessing your data for general service improvements, set the <strong>X-Watson-Learning-Opt-Out</strong> header parameter to <strong>true</strong> for all requests. (Any value other than false or 0 disables request logging for that call.) You must set the header on each request that you do not want IBM to access for general service improvements. </p> 
     <h1 id="error-handling">Error handling</h1> 
     <div class="annotation-block"> 
      <div class="annotation-block--left"> 
       <p> When an error occurs, the <tt>status</tt> attribute of the response will read <tt>ERROR</tt>, and the <tt>statusInfo</tt> attribute will contain a string that describes the error. </p> 
       <h3>Error information</h3> 
       <table class="align-right-1 unwrap-1"> 
        <thead> 
         <tr> 
          <th>statusInfo</th> 
          <th>Description</th> 
         </tr> 
        </thead> 
        <tbody> 
         <tr> 
          <td>invalid-api-key</td> 
          <td>Value of the apikey parameter is invalid</td> 
         </tr> 
         <tr> 
          <td>cannot-retrieve</td> 
          <td>Cannot retrieve the webpage. Contains additional information depending on the reason (see example)</td> 
         </tr> 
         <tr> 
          <td>page-is-not-html</td> 
          <td>Input content is not HTML</td> 
         </tr> 
         <tr> 
          <td>unsupported-text-language</td> 
          <td>The method you are using does not support the language of the source text. If the detected language isn't correct (it usually is for text &gt; 100 characters), you can manually specify the language in the <tt>language</tt> query parameter.</td> 
         </tr> 
        </tbody> 
       </table> 
      </div> 
      <div class="annotation-block--right"> 
       <p class="code-header">Example: inputting a bad URL</p> 
       <pre class=""><code class="lang-bash">
              curl -X POST -d "outputMode=json" -d "url=http://www.ibmc.om" "https://gateway-a.watsonplatform.net/calls/url/URLGetTitle?apikey=%API_KEY%"
            </code></pre> 
       <p class="code-header">Example error response</p> 
       <pre class=""><code class="json">
{
  "status": "ERROR",
  "statusInfo": "cannot-retrieve:operation-timeout:cannot-resolve-dns",
  "usage": "By accessing AlchemyAPI or using information generated by AlchemyAPI, you are agreeing to be bound by the AlchemyAPI Terms of Use: http://www.alchemyapi.com/company/terms.html",
  "url": "http://www.ibmc.om",
  "title": ""
}
            </code></pre> 
      </div> 
     </div> 
     <h1 id="language-support">Language support</h1> 
     <p>The following languages are detectable automatically in each API call, or manually through the Language Detection method. For automatic language detection to work best, it is recommend that you use source text with at least 100 characters.</p> 
     <p>To override language detection, pass the <tt>language</tt> query parameter with your desired language name in lowercase.</p>

      <div class="annotation-block--right"> 
       <p class="code-header"> Overriding language detection </p> 
       <pre><code class="lang-bash">curl -X POST -d "language=spanish" ...</code></pre> 
      </div> 
     </div> 
     <h1 id="linked-data">Linked data</h1> 
     <div class="annotation-block"> 
      <div class="annotation-block--left"> 
       <p> <a href="http://linkeddata.org/" target="_blank">Linked data</a> connects the people, places and things in your content to knowledge databases around the web. AlchemyLanguage supports the following linked data resources in <a href="#entities">Entity</a>, <a href="#concepts">Concept</a>, and <a href="#relations">Relation</a> extraction calls. </p> 
       <ul> 
        <li><a href="http://dbpedia.org" target="_blank">DBpedia</a> - a crowd-sourced community effort to extract structured information from Wikipedia and make this information available on the Web.</li> 
        <li><a href="http://www.freebase.com/" target="_blank">Freebase</a> - a community-curated database of well-known people, places and things.</li> 
        <li><a href="http://www.census.gov/" target="_blank">US Census</a> - quick, easy access to facts about people, business, and geography.</li> 
        <li><a href="http://www.geonames.org/" target="_blank">GeoNames</a> - the GeoNames geographical database covers all countries and contains over eight million placenames that are available for download free of charge.</li> 
        <li><a href="http://www.umbel.org/" target="_blank">UMBEL</a> - the "Upper Mapping and Binding Exchange Layer," it's designed to help content interoperate on the Web.</li> 
        <li><a href="http://www.cyc.com/platform/opencyc" target="_blank">OpenCyc</a> - the gateway to the full power of Cyc, the world's largest and most complete general knowledge base and commonsense reasoning engine.</li> 
        <li><a href="http://www.mpi-inf.mpg.de/yago-naga/yago/" target="_blank">YAGO</a> - a huge semantic knowledge base containing more than 120 million facts about more than 10 million entities.</li> 
        <li><a href="http://musicbrainz.org/" target="_blank">MusicBrainz</a> - an open music encyclopedia that collects music metadata and makes it available to the public.</li> 
        <li><a href="https://www.cia.gov/library/publications/the-world-factbook/" target="_blank">CIA Factbook</a> - provides information on the history, people, government, economy, geography, communications, transportation, military, and transnational issues for 267 world entities.</li> 
        <li><a href="http://crunchbase.com/" target="_blank">CrunchBase</a> - the free database of technology companies, people, and investors that anyone can edit.</li> 
       </ul> 
       <p> In the example entity extraction response shown, "Barack Obama" is identified in DBpedia, Freebase, and YAGO, so the links to those entries appear in the response. </p> 
      </div> 
      <div class="annotation-block--right"> 
       <p class="code-header"> Entity extraction response with linked data </p>

     <h1 id="supported-microformats">Supported microformats</h1> 
     <div class="annotation-block"> 
      <div class="annotation-block--left"> 
       <p>The AlchemyLanguage Microformats function recognizes and extracts the following <a href="http://microformats.org/" target="_blank">microformats</a> data standards:</p> 
       <a href="http://microformats.org/wiki/hcard" target="_blank"><b>hCard</b></a> 
       <ul> 
        <li>FormattedName</li> 
        <li>NameFamilyName</li> 
        <li>NameGivenName</li> 
        <li>NamePrefix</li> 
        <li>NameSuffix</li> 
        <li>OrgName</li> 
        <li>Role</li> 
        <li>Telephone</li> 
        <li>Title</li> 
        <li>Url</li> 
        <li><i>all supported geo properties listed below</i></li> 
        <li><i>all supported adr properties listed below</i></li> 
       </ul> 
       <a href="http://microformats.org/wiki/geo" target="_blank"><b>geo</b></a> 
       <ul> 
        <li>GeoLatitude</li> 
        <li>GeoLongitude</li> 
       </ul> 
       <a href="http://microformats.org/wiki/adr" target="_blank"><b>adr</b></a> 
       <ul> 
        <li>AddrStreetAddress</li> 
        <li>AddrExtendedAddress</li> 
        <li>AddrPostOfficeBox</li> 
        <li>AddrLocality</li> 
        <li>AddrPostalCode</li> 
        <li>AddrCountry</li> 
       </ul> 
       <a href="http://microformats.org/wiki/rel-tag" target="_blank"><b>rel-tag</b></a> 
       <ul> 
        <li>RelTag</li> 
        <li>RelTagLink</li> 
       </ul> 
       <a href="http://microformats.org/wiki/rel-license" target="_blank"><b>rel-license</b></a> 
       <ul> 
        <li>RelLicense</li> 
       </ul> 
      </div> 
      <div class="annotation-block--right">

    <script src="/js/vendor/jquery.min.js"></script> 
    <script>

window.onload = function() {
  reformatCurl();

  // Show URL calls by default
  $('.alchemy-html').css('display','none');
  $('.alchemy-text').css('display','none');
  $('.alchemy-url').css('display','block');
}




function ShouldReformat() {

  var os=0;

  if (navigator.appVersion.indexOf("Win")!=-1) os= 0;
  if (navigator.appVersion.indexOf("Mac")!=-1) os= 1;
  if (navigator.appVersion.indexOf("Linux")!=-1) os= 1;

  return os;
}


// Takes copy/pastable windows-supported curl commands and translates them to mac style
function reformatCurl() {
  if (ShouldReformat()) {
    $('pre[class*="method-curl"] code[class*="lang-bash"] span[class*="hljs-operator"]').before("\\\n");
    $('pre[class*="method-curl"] code[class*="lang-bash"]').html(function(_, html) {
      html = html.replace(/(--data-urlencode)/g, '\\\n$1');
      html = html.replace(/(-F )/g, '\\\n$1');
      html = html.replace(/(-u )/g, '\\\n$1');
      html = html.replace(/(-H )/g, '\\\n$1');
      html = html.replace(/%API_KEY%/g, '$API_KEY');
      return html.replace(/(<span class="hljs-string">"http)/, '\\\n$1');
    })
  }
}

function toggleMethod(scope, input, el) {
  // scope should be the same as the method's h2 id
  // input is "alchemy-[html, url, text]"
  // el should always be "this"

  $('.'+scope+'.inputToggles').children().removeClass('inputSelect');
  el.className += " inputSelect";
  switch (input) {
    case 'alchemy-html':
    $('.'+scope+'.alchemy-text').css('display','none');
    $('.'+scope+'.alchemy-url').css('display','none');
    break;
    case 'alchemy-text':
    $('.'+scope+'.alchemy-url').css('display','none');
    $('.'+scope+'.alchemy-html').css('display','none');
    break;
    case 'alchemy-url':
    $('.'+scope+'.alchemy-html').css('display','none');
    $('.'+scope+'.alchemy-text').css('display','none');
  }

  // important to display after hiding so divs w/ multiple tags will show
  $('.'+scope+'.'+input).css('display','block');

  // Recalculate height offsets for tocify, so menu links highlight properly
  window.toc.calculateHeights();
}
</script>
